- **MCP server — `GET/POST/DELETE /api/mcp`.** Project Minder now embeds a Model Context Protocol server so Claude Desktop and Claude Code can ask conversational questions about token usage, sessions, agents, skills, OTEL telemetry, manual steps, insights, git status, and portfolio stats — and get answers from the same data layer the dashboard reads. Uses SDK 1.29's `WebStandardStreamableHTTPServerTransport` (single Next.js Route Handler dispatching GET/POST/DELETE to a `globalThis`-cached transport, stateless mode, JSON response). ~35 tools registered across 10 domains in `src/lib/mcp/tools/`; ~12 resources (URI-addressable, `minder://projects/{slug}`, `minder://agents/{id}`, etc.) in `src/lib/mcp/resources.ts`. Tools call lib functions directly — no HTTP loopback. Five low-blast-radius writes included (`scan-projects`, `update-project-config`, `toggle-manual-step`, `refresh-catalog`, `refresh-git-status`); dev-server start/stop and `claude-config/apply` deliberately excluded. DNS-rebinding protection pinned to `localhost:4100` / `127.0.0.1:4100`. New raw OTEL query helpers `queryOtelEvents` / `queryOtelMetrics` in `src/lib/db/otelQueries.ts`. Composed lookup helpers `gatherContextOverhead` (`src/lib/contextOverheadComposed.ts`) and `getProjectGitActivity` (`src/lib/projectGitActivity.ts`) extracted so both the API route and the MCP tool share one implementation. 19 new tests across `tests/mcpServer.test.ts`, `tests/mcpTools.test.ts`, and `tests/mcpResources.test.ts` (uses the SDK's `InMemoryTransport` for in-process testing). Client setup documented in `docs/help/mcp-server.md`.
- **Session Detail Wave 7 — Replay scrubber + retry cycle highlights.** Two debugging-grade enhancements to the session detail Timeline tab: (A) **Replay scrubber** — a range slider above the event list lets you scrub through the session's events chronologically, hiding later events to see what the conversation looked like at any earlier point. The slider position shows `N / total` and a Reset button returns to the full view. Pure client-side (no refetch). (B) **Retry cycle highlights** — the timeline now detects Edit/Write → Bash(test) → re-Edit patterns (structural signature of Claude retrying after a failed verification) and highlights all events within such cycles with an amber left border. The scrubber bar shows a `N retry cycles` badge when any are detected. Detection logic lives in the new `src/lib/usage/retryDetector.ts` (`detectRetrySpans`) with 9 tests in `tests/retryDetector.test.ts`.
- **Agent Observatory Wave 6 — Live spend ticker, budget alerts, and rate-limit forecaster.** Three connected features that make session cost actionable on `/agent-view`: (A) **Spending limits config** — `MinderConfig` gains `subscriptionTier` (`pro` | `max5x` | `max20x` | `api`) and `budgets.sessionUsd` / `budgets.dailyUsd`. All four fields are configurable in Settings → Cost → "Spending Limits". (B) **Card budget glow** — when a session's `costEstimate` approaches or exceeds `budgets.sessionUsd`, its Kanban card gains a `box-shadow` ring: amber at 80%, red at 100%. The glow is additive alongside the existing status border so status color still reads clearly. (C) **OS budget notifications** — `useBudgetAlerts` fires a browser `Notification` the first time each session crosses 80% and 100% of the session budget. Uses a `useRef<Map<sessionId, Set<threshold>>>` to ensure each threshold fires at most once per session per page load. Requests notification permission lazily on first alert, not on mount. Pure edge-detection logic extracted into `src/lib/agentView/budgetAlerts.ts` (`computeAlerts`) for unit testability. (D) **Daily spend banner** — a new `SpendBanner` component above the Kanban grid fetches `/api/usage?period=today` (polling every 60s) and shows today's total cost, a progress bar toward the effective daily cap, and a burn-rate projection (`cost / hoursElapsed × 24`). The banner turns amber at 70% of cap, red at 90%. When neither a tier nor a daily budget is configured and today's cost is $0, the banner is hidden entirely. New `src/lib/agentView/tierCaps.ts` defines monthly costs for each subscription tier and exports `getEffectiveDailyCapUsd(tier, dailyUsd)` — explicit `dailyUsd` takes precedence over the tier-derived cap. 15 new tests: 6 in `tests/tierCaps.test.ts` and 9 in `tests/budgetAlerts.test.ts`.
- **Agent Observatory Wave 5 — JSONL-creation watcher for near-instant session discovery.** New `src/lib/agentView/jsonlWatcher.ts` watches `~/.claude/projects/` recursively using Node's built-in `fs.promises.watch` (no new deps) and emits onto the agent-view event bus the moment a new JSONL file appears — cutting worst-case new-session latency from ~21s (6s cache TTL + 15s heartbeat) to ~200ms (debounce). Pure-function `parseJsonlPath(projectsDir, filePath)` extracted for unit testing; 6 tests in `tests/jsonlWatcher.test.ts`. Degrades silently on Linux (recursive watch unsupported) while retaining the existing JSONL-mtime fallback. Wired into `GET /api/agent-view/stream` alongside `startJobRosterWatcher()`.
- **Agent Observatory Wave 4a — Tool failure badge on Kanban cards.** `PostToolUse` hook payloads now carry a normalized `toolFailed` boolean (set at ingest from `tool_response.is_error` or a non-zero `return_code`). When the most recent tool call for a session failed within the last 2 minutes, an amber "⚠ tool err" chip appears in the `AgentCard` footer. The badge clears automatically once a subsequent successful tool event arrives — no sticky state. New `hasRecentToolFailure()` helper in `aggregate.ts`; `LiveAgentSession.lastToolFailed` field added to types. 8 new tests in `tests/hookBuffer.test.ts`.
- **Agent Observatory Wave 4b — Hook installer health indicator + event chips.** The Live Activity section in Settings now lists registered hook events as individual monospace chips (e.g. `PreToolUse`, `PostToolUse`) instead of a plain count, and shows a "Last hook: Xs ago" health line so users can confirm hooks are actually firing without leaving Settings. The timestamp comes from a new `getLastHookReceivedAt()` export on the hook buffer, surfaced via `GET /api/live-activity/install`.
- **Memory Observatory Wave M.4 — Auto-prune / decay recommendations at `/memory/triage`.** Closes the article's gap on memory decay without crossing its "don't auto-delete what the user might still rely on" line: a new page combines Phase 1 telemetry (read count + last-read timestamp) with file age, broken-ref count, and MEMORY.md orphan status to **recommend** (never auto-act) which auto-scope memory files should be archived or deleted. **Scope**: triage operates strictly on `~/.claude/projects/<encoded>/memory/*.md` files — user CLAUDE.md and per-project CLAUDE.md are not move/delete targets because they're authored by the user, not the agent, and MEMORY.md itself is excluded as the index. **Moderate thresholds** (the only built-in profile): archive-candidate if `(never read AND age > 60d) OR (last read > 90d ago)`; consider-deletion if the above PLUS broken refs, broken `@imports`, or orphaned from MEMORY.md. Each row carries its inline reasons (`Never read`, `Last read 47d ago`, `1 broken ref`, `Not in MEMORY.md`). **Actions**: **Archive** moves the file into `<memoryDir>/archive/<filename>` (visible in the Archived section, restorable); **Delete** requires a confirmation step and soft-deletes into `<memoryDir>/.trash/<filename>` for a 30-day window before the per-list-call sweep permanently unlinks expired entries; **Keep 7d/30d/90d** suppresses the row by writing an absPath→ISO map to `.minder.json` under `memoryTriage.suppressUntil`. **Collision handling**: same-named target files in archive/trash get a compact ISO timestamp suffix (e.g. `stale-20260512120241.md`) so prior copies aren't clobbered. The trash dot-prefix (`.trash/`) and the `endsWith('.md')` filter in `listMemoryFiles` keep archived/trashed files out of the main `/memory` listing — they're managed sub-areas, not memory entries. New modules: `src/lib/memory/triageScorer.ts` (pure scoring; 16 tests in `tests/memoryTriageScorer.test.ts`), `src/lib/memory/triageStore.ts` (suppress-map IO via `mutateConfig`), extended `src/lib/scanner/memoryWriter.ts` with `archiveMemoryFile` / `softDeleteMemoryFile` / `restoreFromSubdir` / `listArchivedMemoryFiles` / `listTrashedMemoryFiles` / `sweepTrash` (17 tests in `tests/memoryMover.test.ts` covering atomic-move via `renameWithRetry`, collision suffixes, restore, traversal rejection, the 30d sweep, and the `.md`-only listing filter). New route: `GET /api/memory/triage` returns `{report, archived, trashed}` and best-effort sweeps trash on every call; `POST /api/memory/triage` accepts `{action, projectSlug, fileName, days?}` for the five actions (archive / delete / keep / restore-archive / restore-trash). Restore lifts any active suppression so the file re-appears in the main listing. **Days param clamping**: server clamps `days` to `[1, 365]` and rejects non-finite values outright so a hand-crafted POST can't set a 100-year hold or write an "Invalid Date" into the suppress map. **Six POST actions**: `archive`, `delete`, `keep`, `unsuppress` (lift a Keep hold immediately), `restore-archive`, `restore-trash`. New UI: `/memory/triage` page + `MemoryTriage` component with delete/archive/suppressed/archived/trashed sections, summary banner showing reclaimable bytes, and a two-step Delete confirmation per the M.4 contract. Linked from the sidebar under Sessions next to "Memory seed".
- **Memory Observatory Wave M.1 — Day 1 Memory Seed Generator + M.3 typed authoring at `/memory/seed`.** Closes the article's "Day 1 problem": a freshly-installed Claude Code session walks in already knowing the user's role, stack, repos, and conventions because the seed generator composes five typed memory files from data Project Minder already scans. Generated candidates: `user_role.md` (distilled from `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md`), `user_workstyle.md` (top session categories from JSONL replay via the existing classifier), `reference_repos.md` (active repos with one-line stack summaries), `reference_dev_environment.md` (aggregate framework/ORM/styling signals), and `project_<slug>.md` per top-10 active project (sorted by `lastActivity`). Each candidate carries `derived_from:` provenance in YAML frontmatter and a `seeded: true` flag so the `/memory` browser can surface it later. **Anchor project picker**: user-scope candidates need a target dir; per-project candidates auto-route to their own `memoryDirFor(p.path)`. **3-way diff conflict resolution**: if a candidate's filename exists on disk, the row shows an EXISTS chip and an inline line-by-line LCS diff (existing vs proposed) so the user can pick skip / overwrite / edit-before-promote per row. **M.3 typed authoring (bundled)**: new `src/lib/memory/memoryFrontmatter.ts` parses YAML frontmatter and enforces the prefix↔type contract (`feedback_x.md` must declare `type: feedback`, etc.); `writeMemoryFile()` now validates by default with an opt-out `skipTypeValidation` flag for callers writing untyped scratch files. New modules: `src/lib/memory/seedGenerator.ts` (pure), `src/lib/memory/memoryFrontmatter.ts` (pure validator + composer thin-wrapping the existing `src/lib/indexer/parseFrontmatter.ts`), `src/lib/memory/seedCategoryCounts.ts` (memoized JSONL-mtime-keyed category histogram). The diff renderer reuses `lineDiff` from `src/lib/usage/diff.ts` — same LCS algorithm already used by `MemoryEditor`. New routes: `GET /api/memory/seed?anchor=<projectPath>` returns candidates with on-disk conflict detection, `POST /api/memory/seed` promotes a subset via the existing atomic writer. New UI: `/memory/seed` page + `MemorySeedTray` + `MemorySeedDiff` components, linked from the sidebar under Sessions. 36 new tests across `memoryFrontmatter`, `memorySeedGenerator`, `memorySeedDiff`, plus 5 extensions to `memoryWriter` covering the prefix↔type rejection path.
- **Memory Observatory Phase 1 — Feature D: Budget chips on /memory.** Closes article principle #4 (budget visualization). The summary banner above the scope filters now shows the total bytes-on-disk across every memory file (user CLAUDE.md, project CLAUDE.md, every auto-memory body) compared informationally against the article's 32 KB soft Hermes-style budget; aggregate is always visible with no color tone (the alarm signal lives on the per-row chip below). A "N large files" chip in the banner aggregates how many bodies exceed the 4 KB per-file threshold. Per-row size chips appear next to the display name only when `sizeBytes > 4 KB` — small files stay quiet so the row gutter doesn't get noisy. The existing always-visible `KB` count in the row trailer has been removed; size info only surfaces when it crosses the large-file threshold, matching CONTEXT decision D2. New module `src/lib/memory/budget.ts` exposes three locked constants (`MEMORY_INDEX_LINE_CAP = 200`, `MEMORY_FILE_LARGE_BYTES = 4096`, `MEMORY_TOTAL_BODY_BUDGET_BYTES = 32 * 1024`) plus `budgetTone(value, cap)` (`ok`/`warn`/`alarm` at 80% / 95% thresholds per D3); banner and chips use the shared `formatKB` from `@/lib/utils` for byte rendering. Banner's index-cap tone now goes through the shared `budgetTone` helper instead of inline math — single source of truth for the threshold contract. 7 dedicated tests in `tests/memoryBudget.test.ts` cover constant locks and threshold boundaries (exact-value asserts at 80% and 95% crossover points). **2155 tests passing** (+9 over Feature B's 2146).
- **Memory Observatory Phase 1 — Feature B: Memory read telemetry on /memory.** Closes article principle #2: today's `/memory` shows you what's stored, but never told you which memories Claude Code actually opens vs which it has ignored. The new tracker replays every session JSONL under `~/.claude/projects/*/`, counts `Read({file_path})` tool calls whose target is a memory path (user CLAUDE.md, project CLAUDE.md, or any `~/.claude/projects/<encoded>/memory/*.md`), and stamps a `Read N× · <relative-time>` indicator onto each `/memory` row. Grep/Glob targeting memory directories are deliberately excluded from per-file attribution (their `path` argument is a dir, not a file — they'd need a separate dir-keyed map; they remain visible in `/usage` analytics). New `Unread (30d)` filter chip narrows the list to memories with no recorded reads or whose `lastReadAt` is older than 30 days (server-side filter via `?unread=true` so the cutoff has one source of truth). New module `src/lib/memory/usageTracker.ts` reuses the existing `parseAllSessions()` cache — zero parser modifications, zero double-reads — and writes through to the new SQLite `memory_usage` table for durable storage across restarts. Migration v13 adds `memory_usage(abs_path, read_count, last_read_at, last_updated_at)` plus an index on `last_read_at`. Write-through is best-effort: a DB outage won't break the dashboard (in-memory cache is the read path). New `MemoryFileEntry.usage` field (optional). New endpoints: `GET /api/memory/usage` (raw map, debug/introspection) and `GET /api/memory?unread=true` (filtered entries). 13 dedicated tests in `tests/memoryUsageTracker.test.ts` covering path classification (user/project/auto/case-insensitivity/non-memory rejection) and the aggregator (Read counting, Grep/Glob exclusion, cross-session timestamp picking, lastReadAt monotonicity). **2146 tests passing** (+13 over Feature A's 2133); existing `dbMigrations` assertions bumped to expect schema version 13.
- **Memory Observatory Phase 1 — Feature A: Semantic freshness audit on /memory.** Each memory file's body now gets scanned for source-file refs in prose (`src/lib/foo.ts`, `app/api/users/route.ts`, `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md`) and any candidate that doesn't resolve to a real file shows up as a new `brokenRefs` reason on the `STALE` chip. Closes the gap article principle #1 calls out: today Minder only verifies the structured `@import` directives, not the prose mentions that go stale faster. Extraction is deliberately conservative — only paths with a `/` and one of 16 recognized extensions (ts/tsx/js/jsx/mjs/cjs/md/json/sql/yml/yaml/toml/sh/py/go/rs); triple-fenced code blocks and `http(s)://` URLs are stripped before scanning so example code and GitHub links don't false-positive. Resolution policy: candidate is checked against the memory's parent project first (most refs resolve in one stat); on miss the verifier walks every other scanned project in deterministic order and the first hit wins. `~/foo` candidates expand to the OS homedir and are checked as-is; absolute paths are checked as-is. New `MemoryStaleness.brokenRefs: string[]` field. `StaleChip` tooltip now composes all three reasons (e.g. `2 broken @imports · 3 stale refs · 47d old`); the visible chip stays terse at "stale" so the row layout doesn't shift. New pure-function module `src/lib/memory/staleRefs.ts` with 17 dedicated tests in `tests/memoryStaleRefs.test.ts` covering fence handling, URL stripping, dedup, ext filter, the no-slash guard, home-relative expansion, and the in-flight `(project, candidate)` memoization that keeps a worst-case 60-project × 10-candidate sweep amortized; one new integration test in `tests/memoryDiscovery.test.ts` exercises the wiring through `tryProject`. Existing import cache extended with a `projectsKey` field so a rescan that adds or removes projects invalidates broken-ref verification (file unchanged but project set is different ⇒ recompute). **2133 tests passing** (+18 over Feature C's 2115).
- **Memory Observatory Phase 1 — Feature C: MEMORY.md index awareness.** `/memory` now parses each project's `~/.claude/projects/<encoded>/memory/MEMORY.md` (Claude Code's always-loaded auto-memory index, the "200-line cap" file from Bustamante's *Agent Memory Engineering*) and joins its bullet-link entries against the actual body files in the dir. The summary banner above the scope filters now reports aggregate index health: number of projects with an index, total entries parsed, max line count vs the 200-line cap (amber ≥80%, red ≥95%), orphan count (body files not referenced from any MEMORY.md), and dangling-link count (index entries whose target file is missing). New `indexed` field on `auto`-scope `MemoryFileEntry` is set to `true`/`false` when the project's MEMORY.md is present, `undefined` otherwise (neutral state when there's no index to compare against). New module `src/lib/memory/memoryIndex.ts` is pure-function (parse/count/join/summarize) with 17 dedicated tests in `tests/memoryUserIndex.test.ts`; three integration tests in `tests/memoryDiscovery.test.ts` cover the `tryAuto` wiring (indexSummary emission, `indexed` flag stamping, dangling-link detection). `/api/memory` response shape gains an `indexSummaries` array alongside `entries` — additive, no breaking change for existing consumers. **2115 tests passing** (was 2112, +3 new integration cases on top of 17 new pure-parser cases shared with the index module — net +20 over baseline).
- **Home banner for `permanent-failed` index-DB state.** Surfaces the data-layer state machine's terminal failure (2+ cumulative quarantines unable to recover) as a danger-tinted card above the existing attention strip on `/`. Copy reads "Local index database is unavailable" with the cumulative quarantine count, an instruction to restart the dev server (the state only clears on process exit by design — see `src/lib/data/index.ts:265-270`), and a truncated `code — message` excerpt from `dbHealth.lastError`. Fetched from `/api/health` once on mount; not polled because permanent-failed only resets on process exit so re-probing buys nothing. `transient-failed` (EBUSY / SQLITE_BUSY / EPERM during routine startup races) is deliberately NOT surfaced — the state machine retries those automatically with `[100, 300, 900]ms` backoff and a banner would be alarmist on a recoverable transient.
- **Phase 7.1 — Shared `FindingCard`, `StatCell`, and `severityTokens` extracted from the deferred Phase 7 work.** Closes the consolidation flagged in Phase 7's Risks section ("Steps 1+2+7 deferred to Phase 7.1"). Three atomic commits with byte-for-byte preservation as the discriminator. Typecheck clean, **2094 tests passing** (1 skipped, unchanged from Phase 6.1's baseline — refactor preserves behavior).
  - **`severityTokens` (`src/components/ui/design.tsx`)** — canonical `SeverityTone = "crit" | "high" | "med"` with `{ bg, border, text, icon }` tokens. Three tones is enough for every consumer today; the deferred Phase 7 plan listed five but YAGNI cut it to the reachable set. The mapping table from each consumer's taxonomy is kept local to that consumer (`TONE_BY_SEVERITY: Record<DiagnosisSeverity | WasteSeverity | AuditFindingSeverity, SeverityTone>`).
  - **`FindingCard` (`src/components/ui/FindingCard.tsx`)** — outer shell (tone-tinted bg/border/padding/radius) + header row (icon + tone label + category tag + optional `rightSlot: ReactNode`). Body content flows through `children` so each consumer keeps its own typography for the inner paragraphs — that's what avoided the "expanding the props surface to cover every variant" pitfall the original Phase 7 attempt hit. `DiagnosisPanel` migrated (P0→crit, P1→high, P2→med); `EfficiencyTab` migrated (high→crit, medium→high, low→med). `ClaudeMdAuditPanel` is intentionally NOT migrated — its cards are uniform-neutral by design with severity expressed by the group header, see next bullet.
  - **`StatCell` (`src/components/ui/StatCell.tsx`)** — generic vertical stat tile with `size: "compact" | "feature"` variant (default `compact`). Three sites had near-duplicate `StatCell` functions: `SessionDetailView` + `UsageDashboard` shared the compact treatment (1.25rem mono value, 14×20 padding, body-font label); `StatsDashboard` used the larger feature treatment (1.35rem mono value at weight 700, 12×16 padding, mono label with wider tracking). `accent: "error" | "warn" | "good"` is the superset of all three sites' accent unions. Size tokens live in a `SIZE_TOKENS` Record so the two variants share their identical fields (gap, line-height) and diverge only on the four properties that actually differ. All three sites migrated.
  - **`ClaudeMdAuditPanel` group-header tone coloring** — the panel's section headers ("P0 — Highest priority", "P1 — High priority", "P2 — Medium priority") now consume `severityTokens[TONE_BY_SEVERITY[sev]].text` for their color, so P0 renders red, P1 amber, P2 muted. The cards themselves stay uniform-neutral (per the deliberate scope decision recorded in Phase 7.1's PR rationale) — severity now reads at-a-glance from the header without breaking the visual hierarchy that separates the score row from the findings list.
  - **Visual contract** — byte-for-byte preserved for `DiagnosisPanel`, `SessionDetailView`, `UsageDashboard`, and `StatsDashboard`. `EfficiencyTab` shifts inter-line spacing by 1–2px (its original `marginBottom: 5/4/6` per-row pattern is replaced by the shared card's uniform `gap: 6px` flex-column rhythm) — acceptable consolidation outcome since colors, icons, text, and overall shape are identical. The header-row horizontal gap (originally `gap: 10px` in `FindingRow`, `gap: 8px` in `FindingCard`) is preserved via the optional `headerGap?: number` prop on `FindingCard` — `EfficiencyTab` passes 10, `DiagnosisPanel` accepts the 8px default. `ClaudeMdAuditPanel` gains tone-colored section headers (a visible enhancement, not a regression — severity is now communicated at-a-glance).
- **Phase 6.1 — Live-preview iframe on the Screenshot → React playground.** Closes the deferred follow-up from Phase 6 (live-rendered output for the screenshot-to-code playground at `/config?type=playground`). Typecheck clean, **2092 tests passing** (1 skipped, +19 over Phase 5.1 for the new `tests/previewIframe.test.ts`).
  - **`src/lib/previewIframe.ts`** (pure logic, no I/O) — `stripImports`, `rewriteDefaultExport`, `preparePreviewCode`, `buildPreviewSrcDoc`. The import regex is line-anchored with a negative lookahead `(?!\s*\()` so dynamic `import()` calls in user code aren't matched as module declarations. Multi-line named imports (`import {\n  a,\n  b,\n} from "x";`) are handled via `[\s\S]*?` between `import` and the terminating quoted module path. `<\/script>` sequences in user code are escaped so a string literal containing a closing-script tag doesn't prematurely terminate the babel-typed script in the iframe harness.
  - **`src/components/ScreenshotToCodePreview.tsx`** — renders an `<iframe sandbox="allow-scripts" srcDoc={…}>` with the harness HTML. `srcDoc` is memoized on `code` so the iframe doesn't reload on unrelated state changes. The parent `message` listener matches by `event.source === iframeRef.current?.contentWindow` rather than `event.origin` — sandboxed-without-`allow-same-origin` iframes always report `origin === "null"`, so reference-equality is the only correct filter. Compile and runtime errors are reported to the parent via `postMessage` and surface in a red banner under the preview frame — the in-iframe overlay that an earlier draft considered was removed (per the 6.1c simplify pass) so the preview canvas stays visible alongside the error message.
  - **Why React 18 UMD inside the iframe (not React 19 ESM).** React 19 dropped UMD builds. Using the React 19 ESM bundle would require an `<script type="importmap">` shim and reconfiguring Babel to output ES modules, which complicates the in-iframe compile loop for no visual-fidelity gain on utility-class previews. The React-version mismatch is documented in the playground footer + help doc.
  - **Why stripping imports rather than resolving modules.** `@babel/standalone` doesn't ship a module resolver, so `import React from "react"` throws at runtime. The cleanest fix is a regex pre-pass that nukes all top-level ES `import` lines and exposes `React` + common hooks (`useState`, `useEffect`, `forwardRef`, `memo`, `Suspense`, …) on the iframe's `window`. Imports of other packages in generated code will throw — surfaced via the preview-error banner so the failure is visible, not silent.
  - **Code / Preview toggle in `ScreenshotToCodePlayground.tsx`.** New `OutputPanel` with a custom tab toggle (`Code` default, `Preview` opt-in). Both panels stay mounted via CSS `display: none` — Radix Tabs unmounts inactive content by default, which would tear down the iframe and re-fetch all four CDN scripts on every toggle. The custom toggle preserves the iframe across switches.
  - **Bundle impact: zero.** The iframe loads `@babel/standalone` (~3 MB), React 18 UMD, ReactDOM 18 UMD, and Tailwind v4 browser entirely from CDN inside the sandboxed iframe — none of these scripts enter the parent Next.js bundle. The only new code in the parent build is the ~5 KB preview component + ~3 KB pure-logic module.
  - **Security boundary.** `sandbox="allow-scripts"` without `allow-same-origin` puts the iframe in an opaque origin: it cannot read parent's cookies, localStorage, or DOM, and cannot navigate the parent. CSP was verified empty in `next.config.ts`, so inline-script harness HTML works without a nonce.
  - **Help doc update.** `docs/help/config.md` + `public/help/config.md` gain a new "Screenshot → React Playground" section documenting the provider/model matrix, env-var handling, and the Code/Preview tabs with notes on React 18 / import-stripping / preview-as-approximation framing.
  - **Simplify-pass refinements** (third commit `Phase 6.1c`): (a) `OutputPanel`'s hand-rolled tab buttons replaced with the existing `Seg<T>` primitive in `src/components/ui/design.tsx`; (b) the duplicate `ErrorBanner` in `ScreenshotToCodePlayground` + `PreviewErrorBanner` in `ScreenshotToCodePreview` collapsed into a single shared `ErrorBanner` (with optional `label` prop) lifted into `src/components/ui/design.tsx` — only the two new playground files consume it for now; the 9 other inline error-banner sites can migrate in a separate consolidation pass; (c) the in-iframe error overlay (`#__preview_err`) was dropped — the parent `<ErrorBanner>` is now the single error UX, which keeps the preview canvas visible when a compile/runtime error fires; (d) `rewriteDefaultExport`'s named-fn regex hoisted to module scope to avoid recompiling on every call; (e) `OUTPUT_VIEWS` const drives both the type union and the segmented-control options from one source of truth. Net diff: -54 LOC (134 deletions, 80 insertions across 4 files).
- **Phase 5.1 — Hook toggle parity in ConfigBrowser + project-shared affordance.** Closes the two follow-ups deferred from Phase 5 (ConfigBrowser `HooksList` parity + project-shared toggle decision). Typecheck clean, **2073 tests passing** (1 skipped) — unchanged from Phase 4.1 baseline (this PR is wiring + presentational, no new logic surface).
  - **ConfigBrowser `HooksList` parity.** `/config?type=hooks` now renders the same toggle button + disabled-stash section that `/hooks` has had since Phase 5. `useDisabledHooks` lives inside `HooksList` (not at the `ConfigBrowser` level) so it only fires when the user opens the Hooks tab — matches the existing per-tab gating pattern around `useConfig`. The parent passes a single `onActiveChanged` callback (= `useConfig.refresh`) so a toggle re-fetches both the active list and the sidecar list. Toggle button on each row is gated to `user`/`local` source rows via `isToggleableHookSource`; plugin-bundled rows still render no toggle. `DisabledHooksSection` mounts beneath the rows. Wiring is share-the-state, not a component extraction — both pages keep their own row layouts (the Config tab needs scope+effective badges + `ApplyUnitButton` that `HooksBrowser` doesn't carry).
  - **Project-shared hook affordance.** Project-source rows (those from a git-tracked `.claude/settings.json`) now render a faded **edit settings.json** chip with a tooltip explaining the constraint: hooks are additive in Claude Code (no `disabledHooks` runtime affordance, unlike MCP's `disabledMcpjsonServers`), and `settings.local.json` cannot shadow them. Surfaces the limitation Phase 5 already enforced silently. Lives in `src/components/config/primitives.tsx:ProjectSharedHookChip` so both `/hooks` and `/config?type=hooks` render it identically.
  - **Typed source predicates.** New `isToggleableHookSource` / `isProjectSharedHookSource` predicates in `src/lib/types.ts` (next to `HookSource`). Both render sites use them instead of inline string-equality checks — adding a new `HookSource` member becomes a compile-time prompt rather than a silent miss.
  - **Plan deviation**: the open "git-aware sidecar inside the project" idea from Phase 5's Risks section is **not viable** — confirmed via `src/lib/effectiveConfig.ts:computeEffectiveHooks` (line 106 comment: "Hooks are ADDITIVE in Claude Code"). A project-local sidecar would have no runtime effect because Claude Code has never heard of `.claude/.minder/disabled-hooks.json`. Option (i) from the user-facing decision was selected: honest UX affordance, no fake behavior.
- **Phase 4.1 — Period toggle on the `/agents/[id]` and `/skills/[id]` Usage tab + markdown body renderer.** Closes the two follow-ups deferred from Phase 4.
  - **Period toggle (24h / 7d / 30d / All).** New `?period=` query param on `GET /api/agents/[id]` and `GET /api/skills/[id]`. Default remains `all` so first-load behavior is unchanged. Both DB and file backends honor the filter:
    - **DB path**: `loadAgentUsageFromDb(db, sinceIso?)` + `loadSkillUsageFromDb(db, sinceIso?)` extend the aggregate query with `AND tu.ts >= ?`. `tu.ts` is stored as ISO8601 TEXT in the schema and sorts lexicographically, so the predicate is index-friendly and needs no schema change.
    - **File-parse path**: `groupAgentCalls(turns, sinceMs?)` + `groupSkillCalls(turns, sinceMs?)` skip turns whose timestamp predates the bound (or fails to parse). The shared `parseAllSessions` turn cache is period-blind on purpose — filtering happens after rehydration, not at parse time.
    - **Cost on bounded windows**: `getAgentUsage(period)` skips the per-agent cost merge when `period !== "all"` (cost is computed by a separate JSONL walk that has no period dim). The "Total cost" tile already gates on `costUsd > 0`, so it simply hides rather than reporting all-time cost against bounded invocations.
  - **`src/lib/usage/period.ts`** — thin Phase 4.1 wrappers (`parseUsagePeriod`, `periodSinceIso`, `periodSinceMs`, `DETAIL_PERIODS`) over the **canonical app-wide period helpers** in `src/lib/usage/constants.ts` (`Period`, `VALID_PERIODS`, `validatePeriod`) and `src/lib/usage/periods.ts` (`getPeriodStart`). Phase 4.1's pre-simplify draft minted a parallel `USAGE_PERIODS`/`UsagePeriod`/`isUsagePeriod` vocabulary; the simplify pass folded it into the canonical one and added `"24h"` to `VALID_PERIODS` + `getPeriodStart` so every surface in the app speaks the same vocabulary. `"today"` (calendar midnight) and `"24h"` (rolling) coexist — agent/skill detail uses 24h via `DETAIL_PERIODS` (a `.filter()` over the canonical 5-option list); stats cards / Home / Kanban keep calendar-today.
  - **`ItemUsageBreakdown.tsx`** — gains an optional `period` + `onPeriodChange` + `loading` prop. The toggle renders only when `onPeriodChange` is wired — preserves backwards-compat for any caller wanting a frozen view. Period-aware empty-state copy ("No invocations in the last 24 hours.") replaces the generic "No usage recorded yet." when the filter is active and zero. Body dims to 0.6 opacity during refetch instead of unmounting — avoids the empty-flash between requests.
  - **`AgentDetailView.tsx` + `SkillDetailView.tsx`** — own the `period` state, thread it into the fetch URL and into `ItemUsageBreakdown`. `useEffect` deps go from `[id]` to `[id, period]`. Refetch keeps the prior `data` visible (`loading && !data` skeleton gate) so the header + Overview don't disappear during the swap.
  - **Markdown renderer for Body tab.** The hand-rolled `parseMarkdown` + `inlineToReact` that lived inline in `HelpPanel.tsx` moves to **`src/components/ui/MarkdownRenderer.tsx`** so both the help system and the new BodyTab can share it. The help-system slug routing becomes an opt-in `onLinkClick` prop — HelpPanel passes a delegate that recognizes `*.md` hrefs; BodyTab omits it so links are inert. Same renderer, same look, no new dep (`react-markdown` would have added ~50 KB for a feature the project's own hand-rolled subset already covers).
  - **42 new tests**: `tests/markdownRenderer.test.ts` (15 — block-level + inline coverage of the extracted module), `tests/usagePeriod.test.ts` (15 — `parseUsagePeriod` including the legacy `week`/`month` delegation to `validatePeriod`, both since-helpers, ISO lexicographic-sort sanity check, `DETAIL_PERIODS` subset shape, local-tz calendar-today semantic), `tests/usage/agentParserPeriod.test.ts` (7 — file-parse path with explicit `sinceMs`, including inclusive lower bound + unparseable-timestamp defense), `tests/dataAgentsUsagePeriod.test.ts` (5 — DB path with `sinceIso`, including inclusive lower bound + empty-window).
  - **Plan deviations** (recorded in plan's Risks section update): (1) Filter column is `tu.ts` (the tool_use row's own timestamp), not `sessions.end_ts` as the plan stated — a session that ran for 3 days would otherwise lump every turn into one bucket based on session end time. Per-invocation `tu.ts` matches the UI claim ("invocations in last 24h"). (2) Default period is `all`, not `7d`, so the first-load view is unchanged from Phase 4 — avoids "where did all my invocations go" UX surprise for users who relied on the all-time display.
- **Phase 6 (#238) — Screenshot-to-React MCP server + Config playground.** Convert a UI screenshot into a self-contained React TypeScript component, callable from inside Claude Code (via the bundled stdio MCP server) or directly in the Project Minder UI (via a new "Playground" tab on `/config`). Three vendors supported: Gemini (default), OpenAI, Anthropic.
  - **`src/mcp/screenshot-to-code/index.ts`** — stdio MCP entry. Registers a single tool `convert_screenshot_to_react` with a Zod-validated input schema (`image` base64 required; optional `mediaType`/`framework`/`variant`/`model` overrides). Spawn-time config via env (`SCREENSHOT_PROVIDER`, `SCREENSHOT_MODEL`, `SCREENSHOT_API_KEY_ENV`); request-time keys are read from the named env var only — never persisted to disk.
  - **`src/mcp/screenshot-to-code/providers.ts`** — direct `fetch` adapters for each vendor's documented REST endpoint (Gemini `generateContent`, OpenAI `/v1/chat/completions`, Anthropic `/v1/messages`). No vendor SDKs were added — keeps the bundled MCP server at ~9 KB instead of the ~hundreds of KB three SDKs would pull in.
  - **`src/mcp/screenshot-to-code/prompts.ts`** — prompt template parameterized by framework (`react` inline-styles vs `react-tailwind`) and variant (`minimal` single-component vs `verbose` prop-driven). Plus `cleanCodeBlock()` — strips markdown fences, leading prose, "Here is the component:" preambles, and stray trailing chatter that providers regularly emit despite the "code only" guard.
  - **`scripts/build-mcp-screenshot.mjs`** + **`src/mcp/screenshot-to-code/package.json`** — esbuild bundler that produces `dist/mcp/screenshot-to-code/index.mjs` (`packages: "external"`, ESM, shebang banner). The sub-`package.json` declares the `bin` entry. Wire into Claude Code with `claude mcp add screenshot-to-code -- node /abs/path/to/dist/mcp/screenshot-to-code/index.mjs` (see MANUAL_STEPS.md). New npm script: `npm run build:mcp-screenshot`.
  - **`POST /api/screenshot-to-code`** — proxy that the in-app playground hits. Same provider+prompt+cleanup pipeline as the MCP server. Returns 400 INVALID_BODY, 412 API_KEY_MISSING (with env-var name hint), 413 IMAGE_TOO_LARGE (6 MB cap), 502 PROVIDER_ERROR (or vendor's status code if it's a usable HTTP code).
  - **`ScreenshotToCodePlayground.tsx`** — drag-drop zone + provider/model/framework/variant dropdowns + Convert button + Copy-code button. Mounts as a new "Playground" tab on `/config` next to Settings/Hooks/Plugins/MCP/CI-CD/Keys.
  - **`MinderConfig.screenshotToCode`** — optional `{ provider, model, apiKeyEnvVar }`. Body fields override config; config overrides per-provider defaults. The route deliberately ignores the configured `apiKeyEnvVar` when the body overrides `provider` to something different — using a Gemini key for an OpenAI call would silently 401.
  - **37 new tests** across `tests/screenshotPrompts.test.ts` (13 — buildPrompt branches + cleanCodeBlock against fence/prose/preamble variants), `tests/screenshotProviders.test.ts` (9 — wire format + success + non-2xx for each of the three vendors with mocked `fetch`), `tests/screenshotMcpHandler.test.ts` (8 — `handleCall` tested directly without the stdio transport, with mocked provider), and `tests/screenshotApiRoute.test.ts` (7 — body validation, env-key precondition, body-vs-config priority, ProviderError → status mapping, 413 size cap).
  - **Plan deviations** (recorded in plan's Risks section): (1) `MinderConfig` lives in `src/lib/types.ts` not `src/lib/config/schema.ts` — extended in place. (2) Codebase has no `src/components/config-browser/` subdir — Playground component sits at `src/components/ScreenshotToCodePlayground.tsx`. (3) **Live preview iframe deferred** — the plan called for `@babel/standalone` + Tailwind CDN inside a sandboxed iframe to render the LLM output, but @babel/standalone is ~3 MB and live-rendering arbitrary LLM-generated TSX has many sharp edges (TS-with-JSX compilation, Tailwind class scanning at runtime, runtime sandbox correctness). Shipping just the code-output + Copy-button delivers the core value; users who want a preview can paste into their own dev environment. Captured as a phase-6 follow-up.
- **Phase 5 (#40) — Hook enable/disable via sidecar stash.** Real toggle that survives Claude Code's lack of a `disabled` field for hooks. The Hooks browser at `/hooks` gains an inline `disable`/`enable` button next to each `user`-scope and `local`-scope row, and a "Disabled (N)" section beneath the active list sourced from the new sidecar.
  - **`src/lib/hookToggle.ts`** — pure module: `disableHook({ scope, hookId, projectPath? })` locates the matching command via the existing `makeHookKey()` identity (one shared key with the Wave-5.3 apply layer), removes it from settings, and stashes the original raw JSON object in `~/.claude/.minder/disabled-hooks.json` along with `{ event, matcher?, originalEventIndex, originalHookIndex, matcherGroupExisted, removedAt }`. Pruning cascades: empty matcher group → empty event arr → empty `hooks` key. `enableHook()` reverses the operation, clamping the original indexes to current array lengths and recreating the matcher group when the surrounding tree was emptied. Stashing the raw object (rather than rebuilding from `{type, command, timeout}`) guarantees a byte-equal round-trip.
  - **Lock ordering**: settings → sidecar, consistent across both operations, to avoid cross-chain deadlock against the FIFO-per-path `withFileLock`. `recordPreWrite` snapshots the settings file before every mutation so a misclick is one configHistory restore away.
  - **`POST /api/hooks/toggle`** — `{ action, scope, hookId, projectPath? }`. Status codes: 400 INVALID_BODY/INVALID_SCOPE/PROJECT_PATH_REQUIRED/PATH_NOT_ALLOWED, 404 NOT_FOUND, 409 ALREADY_DISABLED, 422 SETTINGS_MALFORMED. `projectPath` (when supplied for local scope) is allowlisted against the live scan so the route can never write to an arbitrary filesystem path. Successful toggles invalidate `userConfigCache` and the `claude-config` route cache; for `local`-scope toggles the project scan cache is also invalidated, since `scanClaudeHooks` reads each project's `settings.local.json` and the change wouldn't surface in `/api/claude-config?type=hooks` until the 5-min TTL expired otherwise.
  - **`GET /api/hooks/toggle`** — returns sidecar entries whose source settings file still exists on disk (filters out stash entries from deleted/moved projects, since re-enabling one of those would `mkdir` at the stale path).
  - **`HookToggleButton.tsx` + `DisabledHooksSection.tsx` + `useDisabledHooks` hook** — small client primitives. `HookToggleButton` returns null for `plugin` and project-shared `project` sources so the button only renders on toggleable rows. `useHooks()` was extended with a `refresh` so toggle success can re-fetch both lists.
  - **17 new tests** in `tests/hookToggle.test.ts` covering `resolveSettingsPath`, byte-equal round-trip, multi-command matcher (disable c2 of `[c1,c2,c3]` leaves `[c1,c3]`), pruning cascade, recreation of the pruned tree on re-enable, all four error codes, sidecar shape, local-scope round-trip on `settings.local.json`, configHistory snapshot recording, and FIFO serialization of two parallel disables (one wins, the other gets `NOT_FOUND` because the command was already removed from settings).
  - **Plan deviations from spec** (also recorded in plan's Risks section): (1) toggleable scopes are `user` + `local` only; project-shared `.claude/settings.json` rejected because that file is git-tracked and a "personal disable" would dirty the repo for teammates (mirrors `mcpToggle.ts` precedent). Plugin-bundled hooks are also rejected — the user should toggle the plugin instead. (2) `HooksList.tsx` referenced in the plan doesn't exist as a separate file; the toggle button + disabled section are wired into `HooksBrowser.tsx` (the `/hooks` page). The matching `HooksList` inside `ConfigBrowser` (`/config?type=hooks`) was not extended in this phase — same component file, can be a one-line follow-up.
- **Phase 4 (#38) — Per-item detail pages at `/agents/[id]` and `/skills/[id]`.** New routes that render the full body, frontmatter, usage breakdown, and version metadata for any catalog entry.
  - **`/agents/[id]/page.tsx`, `/skills/[id]/page.tsx`** — client pages that decode the URL-encoded catalog id (ids contain colons, e.g. `skill:user:user:bundled:foo`) and mount their respective detail view. `useDocumentTitle` reflects the item id.
  - **`AgentDetailView.tsx`, `SkillDetailView.tsx`** — fetch `/api/agents/[id]` / `/api/skills/[id]` (which already exist), share a `Tabs` layout: `Overview | Body | Usage | Versions`. Distinct headers — agents surface model + tool count; skills surface layout + `userInvocable` + disabled state. 404 path renders an inline back-link to the parent browser.
  - **`CatalogItemDetail.tsx`** — shared building blocks (`DetailHeader`, `OverviewTab`, `BodyTab`, `VersionsTab`) consumed by both detail views. Body is rendered as a preformatted `<pre style={{whiteSpace: "pre-wrap"}}>` block (matches the existing inline preview convention in `AgentsBrowser`). Versions only populates for `marketplace-plugin` provenance; everything else surfaces "Not version-tracked."
  - **`ItemUsageBreakdown.tsx`** — shared usage panel: header tiles (invocations · cost (agents only) · last/first used) + per-project bar chart sorted by invocation count + recent-session deep-links to `/sessions/[id]`. Renders an empty-state when invocations is zero.
  - **`AgentsBrowser`, `SkillsBrowser`**: each row gains an "Open ↗" link in the right-aligned column that navigates to the detail page (with `e.stopPropagation()` so the inline-expand still toggles when the rest of the row is clicked).
  - **`src/lib/catalogDetail.ts`** — pure helpers extracted for testability (`formatFrontmatterValue`, `frontmatterTableEntries`, `versionRows`).
  - **13 new tests** in `tests/catalogDetail.test.ts` covering frontmatter rendering, table-entry filtering (drops `name`/`description` and empty values; preserves `0`/`false`), and version-row construction across all 4 `Provenance` kinds.
  - **Plan deviations from spec** (also recorded in plan's Risks section): (1) Body tab uses `<pre>` preformatted text — the plan referenced an "existing markdown renderer in `ClaudeMdAuditPanel`" that doesn't exist; the codebase has no markdown renderer dep. (2) The 24h/7d/30d period toggle on the Usage tab is deferred — the existing API returns all-time `AgentStats`/`SkillStats` with no period dimension; implementing the toggle requires extending the routes with a `?period=` query param and new DB joins on `sessions.end_ts`, outside this phase's stated file list.
- **Phase 3 (#135) — Context overhead estimator at `/stats`.** Portfolio-wide stacked-bar panel that breaks total context overhead into baseline (3,200 t), MCP servers (~1,250 t/server using a 5-tool × 250-t heuristic), skills (full body bytes / 4 — ceiling estimate, since Claude Code only injects frontmatter descriptors passively), hooks (stringified user + plugin JSON / 4), and user CLAUDE.md (bytes / 4 with `@imports` expanded). The panel also surfaces an **Observed** column — the median first-assistant-turn `cache_create_tokens` across the most recent 30 indexed sessions — and renders an **Unaccounted** row (`max(0, observed − known)`) when the residual gap is positive, capturing sub-agents, conversation turns, and unmodeled sources.
  - **Aggregator (`src/lib/contextOverhead.ts`)**: pure module — `computeContextOverhead(inputs)` → `{ theoreticalMinTokens, knownTokens, observedTokens, unaccountedTokens, sampleSize, rows[] }`. Each `SourceRow` carries a deep-link (`/skills`, `/config?type=mcp`, `/config?type=hooks`, `/memory`) so users can act on the breakdown.
  - **`GET /api/context-overhead`**: composes `getUserConfig()` (portfolio MCP + user/plugin hooks) + `loadCatalog({ includeProjects: false })` (user + plugin skills) + `readUserClaudeMdContent()` + a SQL probe that picks the lowest-`turn_index` assistant turn with non-zero `cache_create_tokens` per session and limits to the most recent 30. No new caches — each upstream input has its own (5-min userConfig / catalog, mtime-keyed memory).
  - **`ContextOverheadPanel.tsx`**: mounted in a new "Context Overhead" section on `/stats` above Telemetry. Stacked horizontal bar (per-source colors), three header tiles (Known / Observed (median) / Unaccounted), and a row list with per-row "Manage in …" links.
  - **13 new tests** in `tests/contextOverhead.test.ts` covering median (4 cases) + breakdown semantics (9 cases: snapshot, unaccounted-row presence, clamp-to-zero, manual-sum within ±10%, "none" detail strings, median-not-mean, `fileBytes === undefined` backwards-compat, disabled-skill exclusion, hook local-metadata stripping).
- **Phase 2 (#193) — Memory file browser at `/memory`.** Replaces the ComingSoon stub with a cross-tier inventory + inline editor that unifies three scopes: user (`~/.claude/CLAUDE.md`), project (`<project>/CLAUDE.md`), and auto-memory (`~/.claude/projects/<encoded>/memory/*.md`).
  - **Discovery (`src/lib/memory/index.ts`)**: `listMemoryFiles({ projects })` walks all three tiers with a 60 s in-module cache. Each entry carries `{ id, scope, projectSlug?, projectName?, absPath, mtimeMs, sizeBytes, preview, stale }`. The `id` is `base64url(absPath)` — opaque + path-traversal safe. Stale heuristic flags `ageOver30d` and `brokenImports[]` (the latter reuses `expandImports` from the audit pipeline so semantics match `ClaudeMdAuditPanel`).
  - **Path-safety allowlist (`src/lib/memory/safety.ts`)**: `classifyMemoryPath(absPath, projects)` returns scope info only when the resolved path is exactly `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md`, a scanned project's `CLAUDE.md`, or an `*.md` file directly inside that project's auto-memory dir (no dotfiles, no subdir traversal). PUT rejects with **400 PATH_NOT_ALLOWED** before any snapshot or write.
  - **`GET /api/memory`** — cross-tier list.
  - **`GET /api/memory/by-id/[id]`** — `{ content, mtimeMs, sizeBytes, scope, projectSlug? }`. Routed under `by-id/` so the existing `/api/memory/[slug]` per-project route stays untouched.
  - **`PUT /api/memory/by-id/[id]`** — body `{ content: string, mtimeMs: number }`. Validates allowlist → enforces 2 MB cap (413 TOO_LARGE) → checks mtime under `withFileLock` (409 MTIME_CONFLICT on drift > 1 ms) → records configHistory snapshot (label `memoryEditor`) → atomic write → invalidates inventory cache and the per-project `scanMemory` cache when the target is auto-tier.
  - **`GET /api/memory/by-id/[id]/snapshot`** — most recent configHistory snapshot for this file, used by the editor's diff view.
  - **`MemoryBrowser.tsx`** — left rail grouped by scope with search, scope chips, and a stale filter; right pane mounts `MemoryEditor.tsx` (view → edit → save → optional diff toggle showing a hand-rolled LCS-based unified diff against the latest config-history snapshot). 409 surfaces a "File changed externally — Reload" banner.
  - **AppSidebar**: `/memory` row no longer carries `comingSoon`.
  - **18 new tests** across `tests/memoryDiscovery.test.ts` (10) and `tests/memoryByIdRoute.test.ts` (8).
- **`GET /api/health`** — lightweight endpoint returning the schema-readiness state-machine snapshot (`{ ok, db: { state, attempts, quarantineRuns, failedAt, lastError } }`). 200 when healthy/initializing, 503 when in transient/permanent failure. No-store cache header.
- **Settings → DB status row** — always-visible footer in the Settings page polls `/api/health` every 15 s and renders state, attempts count, quarantine count, and last error message.

  - **#10 Command palette**: Global `Ctrl+K` (⌘K) overlay reachable from any page. `src/lib/commandPalette.ts` builds a searchable index from all nav routes, scanned projects, recent sessions, and indexed agents. `CommandPalette.tsx` implements the ARIA combobox/listbox pattern (prefix-bonus fuzzy scoring, ↑↓ arrow navigation, Enter select, Escape close). - **Wave 5.2 — Cluster L: four new top-level browsers.** TODOs #152, #154, #156, #237 from `~/.claude/plans/our-to-do-list-has-gentle-cookie.md`.

Virtualized results table with truncation banner at 10,000 rows. CSV (RFC-4180) and JSON export. localStorage query history (max 20, dedup adjacent). Read-only enforcement by `stmt.readonly` bytecode introspection in `better-sqlite3` — catches `WITH … INSERT RETURNING` CTEs that pass a regex.

Extracts title from front-matter or first `# ` heading; tags from front-matter; related session IDs by UUID regex in body. Tag filter, 300ms-debounced search, sort by mtime/title. Status badge (enabled/disabled/blocked).

- **Wave 5.1 — Catalog UX polish (Cluster K).** TODOs #34, #35, #37, #33 (badges + cost) from `~/.claude/plans/our-to-do-list-has-gentle-cookie.md`. No schema migration; no new third-party deps.
  - **Frontmatter lint warnings (#34).** `parseFrontmatter` now returns `warnings: string[]` capturing YAML parse errors and unclosed `---` blocks. `parseWarnings?: string[]` added to `CatalogEntryBase` (agents + skills) and `CommandEntry`. All walkers (`walkAgents`, `walkSkills`, `walkCommands`) propagate warnings from the parser. A small amber `!` chip (`CatalogLintChip.tsx`) renders in the badge cluster of each catalog row (agents, skills, commands); hovering shows the full warning text via native `title=""`.

The commands API route now loads provenance context and also walks plugin commands.
  - **Project agent/skill count badges (#33).** New scanner module `projectCatalogCounts.ts` counts `.md` files in `<projectPath>/.claude/agents/` and `SKILL.md`-bearing dirs in `<projectPath>/.claude/skills/` (no frontmatter parse, fast). `agentCount?` and `skillCount?` added to `ProjectData`. Scanner orchestrator wires counts into each project scan. `ProjectCard` footer shows `ag N` and `sk N` mono pills between the worktree pill and CI badge.
  - **Per-agent cost attribution (#33).** New `agentCost.ts` module walks all JSONL with a two-pass approach: extract Task `tool_use_id → subagent_type` from main-conversation turns, accumulate cost from sidechain assistant turns by matching `parentToolUseID`. No schema migration. `AgentStats` gains `costUsd?`, `inputTokens?`, `outputTokens?`. `getAgentUsage()` runs the sidechain file-parse in parallel with the SQL query and merges cost into rows. `AgentsBrowser` shows a `$N.NN` mono chip when `costUsd > 0`. `UsageTurn` gains `isSidechain?` and `parentToolUseId?`; `parseSessionTurns` / `parseSessionTurnsWithMeta` gain `includeSidechains?: boolean` option (default false, existing behavior unchanged).

- **Wave 4.5 — Efficiency grade badges + portfolio yield (visual follow-ups from Wave 3.2).** TODOs #108 (project-card grade chip) and #133 (portfolio-aggregate yield row) from `~/.claude/plans/our-to-do-list-has-gentle-cookie.md`. Ships the two user-visible surfaces that were explicitly de-scoped from Wave 3.2 to keep that wave focused on detector logic — all underlying analytics were already in place.
  - **Project-card efficiency grade chip.** Each project card now displays an A–F grade pill in the attention-signals row, computed by `runWasteOptimizer` for every project that has Claude sessions. Grade is loaded lazily via a new `efficiencyGradeCache` singleton (mirrors `gitStatusCache` pattern: background worker, batch-5 processing, 5-min TTL, `globalThis` lifecycle). Cards initially render without a chip; chips fade in as grades arrive over the first ~5 seconds. Color coding: A = green, B = blue, C = neutral, D = amber, F = red. Compact-card variant shows a small grade letter in the inline chip strip. Projects with `sessionCount === 0` are skipped entirely. New API route `GET /api/efficiency-grades` serves the `{ [slug]: grade }` map; `useEfficiencyGrades` hook polls every 5 s and stops when all queued projects have resolved.

Displays yield rate %, productive / reverted / abandoned session counts, and total sessions. Per-project yield chips (`NN%↑`) appear on each row in the By Project breakdown when yield data is available. Yield is computed in `generateUsageReport` via `augmentPortfolioYield`, which runs `computeProjectYield` across all projects in `Promise.all` using the already-cached scan. Gated by `getCachedScan()` so the aggregator never triggers a fresh filesystem scan — a no-op on cold loads.
  - **`computeProjectYield` shared helper** (`src/lib/usage/computeProjectYield.ts`). Extracted from the inline `computeYield` block in `src/app/api/projects/[slug]/efficiency/route.ts`. Both the efficiency route and the aggregator now call the same helper, eliminating the duplicate implementation.

All 1136 tests pass; typecheck clean.

- **Wave 4.2 — Resume anomaly + facets + thinking + turn latency + version history (Cluster I).** TODOs #127, #177, #181a, #181b, #187 from `~/.claude/plans/our-to-do-list-has-gentle-cookie.md`. DB schema v6 (5 new columns); DERIVED_VERSION bumped to 6.
  - **Facets scanner** (`src/lib/scanner/claudeFacets.ts`). Reads `~/.claude/usage-data/facets/<sessionId>.json` (Claude Code's per-session qualitative self-rating). mtime-based file cache. Missing file → null ("No feedback recorded" in UI). Malformed JSON → explicit throw (never silent). `getSessionFacets(id)` + `getFacetsAggregate(ids[])` with distribution counts for outcome, helpfulness, satisfaction, friction, and session type. New **Feedback** tab on session detail (`FeedbackPanel.tsx`). New **Feedback** aggregate section on `/usage` (`FeedbackAggregate.tsx`). API routes: `GET /api/sessions/[id]/feedback` (per-session, 404 when absent) and `GET /api/feedback` (aggregate, 2-min `globalThis` cache, period + project filters).
  - **Thinking-block on-demand rendering** (#181a). `turns.text_offset` records the byte position of each assistant turn in the JSONL; `src/lib/data/thinkingContent.ts` resolves this offset, reads one JSONL line, and extracts `type:"thinking"` content blocks (capped at ~3000 chars). `SessionTimeline` lazily fetches `/api/sessions/[id]/thinking?turnId=N` when a thinking event is expanded under DB mode. Loading state renders "Loading thinking content…"; missing-content renders "Thinking content unavailable for this turn." (no silent skip). `has_thinking` column added to `sessions` and surfaces as a chip on session rows.
  - **Turn-duration badges** (#181b). `system.subtype:turn_duration` JSONL events record the wall-clock milliseconds for the preceding assistant turn. The parser walks backward to the nearest preceding assistant entry (the `parentUuid` field points at the preceding `stop_hook_summary` hook, not the assistant — this walk-back is the correct attachment). `turn_duration_ms` stored on `turns` rows and rendered as a duration badge (`2.3s` / `4m12s`) on assistant events in the session timeline.
  - **Resume anomaly detection** (#127). `src/lib/usage/resumeAnomaly.ts`: for each `compact_boundary` timestamp, partitions assistant turns into 20-turn pre/post windows, computes pre-window median output tokens, flags if any post-window turn exceeds `RESUME_OUTPUT_SPIKE_RATIO=10×` the median. Also flags `cacheCreateTokens > 5000` coincident with flat cache reads (cache rebuild spike). If `isBuggyVersion(cliVersion)` (CLI 2.1.69–2.1.89 prompt-cache bug), appends that reason. Wired into `diagnoseSession` as two new categories: `"buggy-cli-version"` (P1, upgraded to P0 when anomaly present) and `"resume-anomaly"` (P1). New chips on session rows: `resume anomaly` (amber warn) and `thinking` (muted). `has_resume_anomaly` column on `sessions` computed during ingest.
  - **Version history panel** (#187). Collapsible CLI version table on `/usage`. Groups sessions by `cli_version` (most-frequent `version` value in the JSONL, computed during ingest). Columns: version, session count, first seen, last seen. Rows in the 2.1.69–2.1.89 buggy range get a `buggy` badge. `cli_version` stored on `sessions`; `versionDetector.ts` is the single source of truth for the range.
  - **DB schema v6 migration.** Six new columns: `has_thinking` (sessions), `cli_version` (sessions), `has_resume_anomaly` (sessions), `compact_boundary_count` (sessions), `turn_duration_ms` (turns), `has_thinking` (turns). Idempotent `PRAGMA table_info` guards per established v5 pattern.
  - **`parseSessionTurnsWithMeta`** — sibling to `parseSessionTurns`, returns `{ turns, meta }` where meta carries `compactBoundaries`, `cliVersion`, and `hasThinking`. Consumed by ingest, quality route, and resume-anomaly detector. `parseSessionTurns` signature unchanged.
  - **Tests** — 7 new test files: `turnDuration.test.ts`, `cliVersionDetection.test.ts`, `thinkingBlocks.test.ts`, `thinkingContent.test.ts`, `versionDetector.test.ts`, `resumeAnomaly.test.ts`, `claudeFacets.test.ts`. All 1100 tests pass; typecheck clean.
- **Wave 4.1 — Subagent meta intelligence + session handoff + workflow patterns + handoff doc.** Cluster H of the work-back plan in `~/.claude/plans/our-to-do-list-has-gentle-cookie.md` (TODOs #125, #129, #131, #170). Adds session intelligence: canonical subagent descriptions from `.meta.json`, per-session mechanical-fact extraction with compaction fidelity scoring, cross-session Bash-sequence pattern detection, and a one-click markdown handoff doc generator.
  - **`subagentMeta` scanner module** (`src/lib/scanner/subagentMeta.ts`). Reads `~/.claude/projects/<project>/<session>/subagents/agent-*.meta.json` files and returns a `Map<description, SubagentMeta>` keyed by canonical description string. Tolerates missing directories and malformed JSON per-file. `readSubagentMetaSync` variant for the synchronous DB path. `categorize(description)` derives a `SubagentCategory` verb chip from the leading verb of the description: `fix`/`find`/`query`/`research`/`check`/`create`/`other`.
  - **Subagent enrichment** — both the file-parse path (`claudeConversations.ts`) and DB path (`sessionDetailFromDb.ts`) now merge `.meta.json` data onto `SubagentInfo`, populating `category`, `metaTurnCount`, and `metaSourced`. Parity contract maintained: both paths produce identical `SubagentInfo[]` for the same session. The existing 200-char prompt slice remains as fallback when no `.meta.json` exists.
  - **Category chips in session Subagents tab** (`SessionSubagents.tsx`). Verb-derived chips rendered between the type label and the sequence number: red for `fix`, blue for `find`/`query`/`research`, amber for `check`, green for `create`, muted for `other`.
  - **`sessionHandoff` module** (`src/lib/usage/sessionHandoff.ts`). `extractHandoffFacts(turns)` — files modified (from write/edit ops), files read, git commits (both `-m "..."` and HEREDOC forms), key commands (non-trivial Bash, length > 4 tokens). `readCompactionSummary(jsonlPath)` reads the first `compact_boundary` / `compact_summary` record from the JSONL. `scoreCompactionFidelity(facts, summary)` token-overlap scores the LLM-generated compaction against the mechanical facts; flags < 60% as low fidelity with a list of up to 10 missing facts.
  - **Handoff tab on session detail** (`HandoffPanel.tsx`). Three-column grid: Files Modified, Git Commits, Key Commands. Fidelity card below when the session was compacted. "Generate handoff doc" button opens the doc modal.
  - **`sessionHandoffDoc` module** (`src/lib/usage/sessionHandoffDoc.ts`). `generateHandoffDoc(input)` renders a markdown brief at four verbosity levels: `minimal` (task + state + counts), `standard` (+ last 10 turns + full fact lists), `verbose` (+ last 20 turns + commit bodies + fidelity callout), `full` (entire transcript + all facts + tool counts).
  - **Handoff doc modal** (`HandoffDocModal.tsx`). Verbosity dropdown (4 options), Copy + Download `.md` buttons, scrollable `<pre>` preview. Re-fetches on verbosity change.
  - **`workflowPatterns` module** (`src/lib/usage/workflowPatterns.ts`). `detectWorkflowPatterns(input)` fingerprints Bash binary sequences (n-grams of length 2, 3, 4) cross-session. Filters to patterns appearing in ≥ 3 sessions; skips all-identical windows (e.g., `git→git→git`). Suggests kebab-case skill names and fuzzy-matches against the skills catalog (token overlap ≥ 2). Output capped at 50 patterns sorted by session count.
  - **Patterns tab on project detail** (`PatternsPanel.tsx`). Lists recurring patterns with binary chips, session count, run count, and suggested or matched skill name.
  - **`GET /api/sessions/[sessionId]/handoff?verbosity=...`** — returns `{ facts, fidelity, doc, meta }`. 5-min `globalThis` cache keyed on `sessionId:verbosity` with JSONL-mtime invalidation. 400 on unknown verbosity, 404 on missing session.
  - **`GET /api/projects/[slug]/patterns`** — returns `{ patterns, totalSessionsConsidered, totalBashCalls, meta }`. Same 5-min + mtime cache pattern as the efficiency and hot-files routes.
  - **`<Modal>` UI primitive** (`src/components/ui/modal.tsx`). Backdrop click, Escape-to-close, focus trap (Tab/Shift+Tab), scroll-lock. `role="dialog" aria-modal="true"`. No external dependencies.
  - **`extractBashCommands(turn)` promoted to `shellParser.ts`**. Replaces inlined loop at `aggregator.ts:141-146`; reused by `sessionHandoff.ts` and `workflowPatterns.ts`.
  - **`filterCommitsInInterval` added to `git.ts`** — filters `CommitMeta[]` by author timestamp range without additional shell calls.
  - **`SkillEntry.description`** now surfaced from frontmatter (`walkSkills.ts`); consumed by workflow-pattern skill-matching.
  - **Tests** — `tests/subagentMeta.test.ts` (8 cases), `tests/sessionHandoff.test.ts` (12 cases including 3 compact_boundary JSONL shapes), `tests/sessionHandoffDoc.test.ts` (4 snapshot cases, one per verbosity), `tests/workflowPatterns.test.ts` (26 cases). All passing; typecheck clean.
- **Wave 3.3 — File activity + hot files + coupling arc.** Cluster G of the work-back plan in `~/.claude/plans/our-to-do-list-has-gentle-cookie.md` (TODOs #88, #121, #212). Adds cross-session file intelligence to the project detail page and a compact edit-count stat to session rows.
  - **`fileActivity` module** (`src/lib/usage/fileActivity.ts`). `extractFileEdits(turns)` mirrors `extractFileOp()` in the DB ingest path exactly — only `args.file_path` is consulted, never `args.path` or `args.notebook_path`. `extractWriteEdits(turns)` is a write-class subset (write / edit / delete; excludes Read ops) used by both downstream modules.
  - **`fileTracker` module** (`src/lib/usage/fileTracker.ts`). `buildHotFiles(turns, limit=50)` aggregates write-class ops per file path, tracking total edit count, session count, last-edit timestamp, and per-type op breakdown. Returns `HotFilesResult` with the ranked `HotFile[]` list plus `totalFiles` and `totalEdits` for summary display.
  - **`fileCoupling` module** (`src/lib/usage/fileCoupling.ts`). `buildFileCoupling(turns, minCoOccurrences=2, limit=100)` computes co-editing frequency between file pairs across sessions. Uses `\0`-joined canonical pair keys (alphabetically sorted) to ensure `a+b === b+a`. Jaccard-like strength = coOccurrences / max(sessionsA, sessionsB). Per-session file cap of 200 prevents O(n²) blowup on broad refactor sessions.
  - **`GET /api/projects/[slug]/hot-files`**. On-demand, 5-min `globalThis` TTL with mtime invalidation. Same project-matching and session-parsing pattern as the efficiency route.
  - **`GET /api/projects/[slug]/file-coupling`**. Same pattern; accepts `?min=N` query param (default 2) to adjust the co-occurrence threshold. Cache key includes the threshold so changing `min` yields fresh data.
  - **`<HotFilesPanel>` component** (`src/components/HotFilesPanel.tsx`). Summary strip (unique files edited, total edit ops, sessions analysed) + ranked bar list for hot files + co-edited pairs section with Jaccard strength percentages. Both sections show empty-state messages when data is absent.
  - **`ProjectDetail` Hot Files tab**. Added `"hot-files"` to `TabKey` and the tab array; gated on `hasSessions` (same gate as Efficiency). Tab placed immediately after Efficiency.
  - **`SessionsBrowser` compact edit stat**. Each session row now shows an inline "N edits" chip (pencil icon) derived from `toolUsage.Write + Edit + MultiEdit + NotebookEdit`. Hidden when zero so clean read-only sessions don't show `0 edits`.
  - **Tests** — 7 cases in `tests/fileActivity.test.ts` (all ops extracted, user turns skipped, missing/wrong-key args dropped, MultiEdit+NotebookEdit handled, turnIndex populated), 7 cases in `tests/fileTracker.test.ts` (ranking, session dedup, ops breakdown, Read exclusion, limit, lastEditTs, empty input), 8 cases in `tests/fileCoupling.test.ts` (pair detection, threshold, Jaccard math, canonical ordering, per-session dedup, Read exclusion, limit, empty input). All tests pass, typecheck clean.
- **Wave 3.2 — Waste optimizer + session yield + self-correction rate.** Cluster F of the work-back plan in `~/.claude/plans/our-to-do-list-has-gentle-cookie.md`. Surfaces three new analytics behind a single new "Efficiency" tab on each project's detail page plus a small column add to `/usage`'s model breakdown.
  - **`wasteOptimizer` module** (`src/lib/scanner/wasteOptimizer.ts`, TODO #108). Pure transform over `{ turns, configuredMcpServers, agents, skills }` returning an A–F grade plus up to 5 findings: junk-directory reads (`node_modules/`, `.git/`, `dist/`, `build/`, `.next/` — matched against both forward-slash and Windows-backslash path separators), duplicate reads (3+ distinct sessions reading the same file with no intervening Edit/Write), unused MCP servers (configured under any scope but never invoked as `mcp__server__*`), ghost capabilities (indexed agents/skills with zero `Task`/`Skill` invocations on this project — gated to only fire when SOME capabilities have been used so a never-Task'd project doesn't get blamed for its catalog), and low read/edit ratio (sessions where Edit+Write count exceeds Read by >3×). Severity-by-volume thresholds documented inline; A–F roll-up follows TODO #108's spec exactly (A: 0 findings or all low; B: 1–2 medium; C: 3+ medium; D: 1+ high; F: 2+ high or >8 total).
  - **`yieldAnalysis` module** (`src/lib/usage/yieldAnalysis.ts`, TODO #133). Classifies each project session as Productive / Reverted / Abandoned by overlapping the session's [start, end] interval (assistant turn timestamps + 5-min grace at both ends) with the main-branch commit log. Revert detection is text-based on the standard `Revert "<subject>"` form — body-line `This reverts commit <sha>` matching is deliberately not implemented (would require pulling commit bodies, multi-MB on long-lived repos; the subject form catches the common case and produces a strictly conservative metric). Yield rate = productive / total; dollars-per-shipped-commit = total session cost / non-reverted commit count when cost data is available, else `null`. New helpers in `src/lib/scanner/git.ts`: `detectMainBranch` (origin/HEAD → main → master) and `readBranchCommits` (8 s timeout + 16 MB maxBuffer for long-lived repos; bounded by `--since=<earliest-session>` from the caller).
  - **`selfCorrection` module + aggregator wiring** (`src/lib/usage/selfCorrection.ts`, TODO #110). Phrase-based scan over assistant turn text: `my mistake`, `I was wrong`, `I apologize/apologise`, `let me reconsider`, `I made an error`, `I need to correct` — plus `actually,` only when sentence-anchored (start of text or after `.!?` + whitespace) to suppress the noisiest of the seven phrases. Per-session dedup so retry loops can't inflate the count. Aggregated per *primary model* (most assistant turns in the session); rate = correctedSessions / sessionsAsPrimary. Surfaced as new `selfCorrectionRate` + `sessionsAsPrimary` fields on `ModelCost`; `/usage`'s By Model rows now show `· NN% self-corr` when populated. The "primary model" attribution caveat is documented in the field's JSDoc — a 90%-Opus session whose single corrected turn ran on Haiku still attributes to Opus, since the metric tracks the model the user *ran the session on*.
  - **`GET /api/projects/[slug]/efficiency` route**. On-demand, 5-min `globalThis` TTL keyed by slug. Loads sessions for the project via `parseAllSessions` (filtering by `projectSlug`), runs the waste optimizer with the project's MCP set + a project-scoped catalog filter from `loadCatalog({ includeProjects: true })`, computes yield via `detectMainBranch` + `readBranchCommits` (bounded by the earliest session timestamp − 1 day), and returns `{ slug, waste, yieldReport, generatedAt }`. Yield falls back to `{ unavailable: true, reason }` when the repo has no detectable main branch or session data is missing — surfaces in the UI as an explanatory line rather than blank stats.
  - **`<EfficiencyTab>` component** (`src/components/EfficiencyTab.tsx`). New tab on `ProjectDetail`, gated to projects with at least one Claude session (same gate as the existing Sessions tab). Renders the A–F grade pill in a header strip with severity-tinted finding cards (high/medium/low; reuses the same color tokens as `<DiagnosisPanel>`). Yield section shows 5 stat boxes (Productive / Reverted / Abandoned / Yield Rate / $/Shipped Commit) plus a one-line interpretive note. Lazy-fetches on tab activation; loading + error states are explicit so a slow `git log` never produces a blank panel.
  - **Tests** — 29 cases in `tests/wasteOptimizer.test.ts` (each detector's positive / negative / severity-escalation paths + Windows backslash handling + ghost-capability noise floor + grade rollup table for all 6 buckets + sort order), 13 cases in `tests/usage/yieldAnalysis.test.ts` (interval-builder behavior, three classification outcomes, threshold edge case, dollars-per-shipped-commit math, empty inputs), 8 cases in `tests/usage/selfCorrection.test.ts` (each phrase + sentence-anchored `actually,` + per-session dedup + multi-session rate + user-turn exclusion + aggregator integration). 890 tests pass (1 skipped), typecheck clean.
  - **Out of scope**: project-card grade badge from TODO #108, portfolio-aggregate yield row on `/usage`, and the fuse-walks refactor (`tests/usage/sessionQuality.test.ts`'s 5-walk consolidation noted in TODO.md). All three are in TODO.md; the plan's section 3.2 doesn't include them. Following plan-scope discipline.
- **Wave 3.1 — Cache + compaction + tool-failure detectors + session diagnosis panel.** Cluster E of the work-back plan in `~/.claude/plans/our-to-do-list-has-gentle-cookie.md`. The `sessions.has_compaction_loop`, `sessions.has_tool_failure_streak`, `sessions.max_context_fill`, `sessions.cache_hit_ratio` columns and `turns.context_fill` were pre-allocated in v1 of `schema.sql` (P2a foundation) but never written; this wave finally populates them, drives a one-time re-parse via the DERIVED_VERSION 4→5 bump, and exposes the data through new badges and a Diagnosis tab.
  - **`sessionQuality` module** (`src/lib/usage/sessionQuality.ts`). Pure functions over `UsageTurn[]`: `computeCacheStats` (hit ratio + dollar `rebuildWasteUsd` per the Clauditor "hidden waste" formula, computed per-turn so per-model pricing stays accurate), `detectCompactionLoops` (consecutive turn pairs with <10% input variance and >75% fill, per Clauditor's heuristic; runs are merged so a sustained loop reports as one finding), `detectToolFailureStreaks` (greedy non-overlapping scan for windows of 5+ consecutive evaluable turns where >50% carry error markers, with the documented first-6-turns grace). `getModelContextWindow` honors the `[1m]` suffix Claude Code uses for the 1M-context Sonnet 4.x SKU and warns once per unknown model rather than silently dividing by 200K. `computeSessionQuality` runs all detectors plus the cheap `maxContextFill` scan in a single pass; `turnContextFill` exposes the per-turn fill ratio used at ingest write time.
  - **`sessionDiagnosis` module** (`src/lib/usage/sessionDiagnosis.ts`). Implements TODO #106's 8-category taxonomy: cache TTL expiry (>5-min inter-turn gap, capped to skip "I went home" breaks via a 12-hour upper bound), cache thrash (≥3 cache_creation spikes within a 5-minute sliding window), context bloat (any turn >60% fill — suppressed when near-compaction also fires for the same session so advice doesn't double up), near-compaction (any turn >83%), compaction-loop (delegates to sessionQuality), tool-failure streak (delegates to sessionQuality), high-idle (sum of inter-turn gaps capped per gap by the same 12h ceiling), context-dominated (≥30% of assistant turns spent ≥10× more on input than output, with a 50K minimum input gate so small turns don't trip it). Outcome inference layered on top: `stuck` when persistent failure or compaction-loop signal is present, `abandoned` when last turn is user, `partial` when last assistant turn carries an API error, `completed` otherwise. `topAdvice` returns up to three findings ordered by estimated dollar impact (tied severity → P0 > P1 > P2 → declaration order).
  - **DB ingest writes the long-pre-allocated columns** (`src/lib/db/ingest.ts`). `readJsonlSession` now calls `computeSessionQuality(allUsageTurns)` after one-shot detection and stamps `hasCompactionLoop` / `hasToolFailureStreak` / `maxContextFill` onto `ParsedSession`; per-turn `contextFill` populated via `turnContextFill`. Both the full-session INSERT and the tail-append UPDATE write the new columns. The tail path re-runs detectors over old + new combined turns so a long session that develops a streak after the initial reconcile still flips correctly.
  - **DERIVED_VERSION 4 → 5** (`src/lib/db/derivationVersion.ts`). Existing rows have the new columns at default 0/NULL because schema.sql v1 already created them; the bump drives a one-time full re-parse so SessionsBrowser badges and the Diagnosis tab agree across the corpus. No read-side gate — pre-reconcile, badges simply don't render and Diagnosis is computed on demand from the JSONL, so degraded UX never produces wrong numbers.
  - **File-parse path computes the same flags** (`src/lib/scanner/claudeConversations.ts`). `scanSessionFile` now populates token fields on the existing `lightTurns: UsageTurn[]` (previously zeroed) and runs `computeSessionQuality` after the existing one-shot pass, surfacing `cacheHitRatio` / `maxContextFill` / `hasCompactionLoop` / `hasToolFailureStreak` on the returned `SessionSummary`. Identical badges render whether `MINDER_USE_DB=1` or `=0`.
  - **`GET /api/sessions/[sessionId]/quality` route**. Loads `UsageTurn[]` via `loadSessionTurnsBySessionId` (a new path-traversal-safe single-session resolver in `parser.ts` that walks `~/.claude/projects/<dir>/<sessionId>.jsonl` and reuses the `FileCache` for repeat hits) and returns the full `DiagnosisReport`. Uses file-parse regardless of `MINDER_USE_DB` — `loadSessionDetailFromDb`'s documented divergences (no thinking blocks, collapsed `text_preview`, dropped sidechain entries) weaken the diagnosis signal too much to trust. Documented in the route's header comment so a future DB-native refactor knows what gaps to close first.
  - **`<DiagnosisPanel>` component** (`src/components/DiagnosisPanel.tsx`). Lazy-fetches on tab open. Header strip surfaces outcome / cache hit / cache waste (with "saved" inversion when negative) / peak fill / total idle. Top-advice block renders the model's prioritized 3-item list. Findings render as severity-tinted cards with category, finding sentence, advice sentence, and approximate USD impact when calculable. Empty-state surfaces a green "looks healthy" callout instead of nothing. Wired into `SessionDetailView` as a new `Diagnosis` tab — added unconditionally so a clean session still surfaces the healthy-state confirmation.
  - **SessionsBrowser quality badges** (`src/components/SessionsBrowser.tsx`). Three new chips on each row: `<NN>% cache` (green ≥70% / neutral 50–70% / amber <50% — Clauditor's >70% benchmark), `compaction loop` (red), `tool fail streak` (red). All three render only when the corresponding field is populated, so pre-reconcile sessions or those without cache activity simply don't show them.
