  - **Tests** — 25 cases in `tests/usage/sessionQuality.test.ts` (model-window resolution incl. `[1m]` suffix and unknown-model warn-once, cache stats with mixed activity / null / negative-waste cases, compaction-loop detection with high/low fill and high/low variance, **explicit positive + negative regressions for the cache-aware-fill semantic** — heavily-cached healthy sessions correctly stay below the loop threshold; only sessions where `input_tokens` (uncached new content) stays high fire the loop, streak detection with grace, sub-threshold rate, error markers near `toolResultText`'s 2000-char truncation boundary, mixed assistant `isError` + user `toolResultText` errors, `computeSessionQuality` bundled output) and 14 cases in `tests/usage/sessionDiagnosis.test.ts` (clean session emits zero findings, near-compaction triggers and suppresses context-bloat, mid-band fill emits context-bloat alone, cache-TTL gap counting, cache-thrash sliding-window run detection, compaction-loop wiring, stuck-outcome inference from long failure streak, abandoned vs completed outcome rules, topAdvice cap). Two pre-existing version-pinned tests in `tests/dbIngest.test.ts` updated for DERIVED_VERSION 5. **833 tests pass (1 skipped), typecheck clean.**
  - **Browser-verified UX**: tested live at `localhost:4100/sessions` and on a session-detail Diagnosis tab. SessionsBrowser cache-hit chips render across the full session list. Diagnosis tab on a clean cached session correctly shows outcome=Completed with low fill, surfaces real cache-TTL/cache-thrash/high-idle findings, and does NOT false-positive on near-compaction/compaction-loop/context-dominated. An earlier draft summed `input + cache_read + cache_creation` for fill, which produced 317% values and false stuck-outcome reports on healthy heavily-cached sessions; reverted to the spec semantic (`input_tokens / window`) where high values mean "cache is failing per-turn." Two regression tests pin the corrected behavior.
  - **Post-PR-bot-review fixes (#63 review pass; Codex + Copilot)**:
    - **`parseSessionTurns` strict mode**: added `{ strict?: boolean }` option. Default (legacy sweep behavior) swallows `fs.readFile` failures as `[]`; `strict: true` propagates them. The diagnosis path now passes `strict: true` so a permissions error or mid-stream read failure escalates to HTTP 500 instead of producing a misleading green "looks healthy" panel. Per-line `JSON.parse` errors are still soft-skipped regardless — partial reads of a corrupted JSONL are still useful for diagnosis. **Reviewer-flagged**: Codex P1 + Copilot — H1's premise that `parseSessionTurns` would throw was wrong; the function tolerated read failures.
    - **Non-ENOENT readdir failures throw `SessionTurnsLoadError`**: when `~/.claude/projects` exists but is unreadable (EACCES, EIO, EPERM), the loader now throws instead of returning `null` (which the route was mapping to 404). Real misconfigurations now surface as 500 with the operator's log line. ENOENT (no Claude Code on this machine) still returns null → 404 since that's a legitimate "no sessions" state. **Reviewer-flagged**: Codex P2 + Copilot.
    - **`DiagnosisPanel` Peak Fill 0% rendering**: changed `formatPct(report.maxContextFill || null)` → `formatPct(report.maxContextFill)`. The `|| null` coerced a legitimate `0` to `null`, rendering `—` instead of `0%`. Affected sessions where no assistant turn had positive `input_tokens` (some short sessions, all-failed sessions). **Reviewer-flagged**: Copilot.
    - **`pickTopAdvice` lexicographic ordering**: rewrote from additive `impact + SEVERITY_RANK` (which made severity dominate impact almost entirely — a $0 P1 outranked a $300 P2 because realistic impact magnitudes never exceeded the 1000 severity gap) to honest lexicographic ordering: severity tier first (P0 → P1 → P2), then estimated impact within tier, then declaration order. Matches user UX (see all P0 findings before any P2 regardless of dollar value) and the corrected behavior is now pinned by a new test. **Reviewer-flagged**: Copilot.
    - **Synthetic-model parity in file-parse `lightTurns`**: `scanSessionFile` now skips assistant entries with `model === "<synthetic>"` or empty model when building the `lightTurns: UsageTurn[]` projection that feeds `computeSessionQuality`. Both `parseSessionTurns` and DB ingest skip synthetic turns; without this fix, the file-parse path's quality output would diverge from the DB path's for any session containing them. **Reviewer-flagged**: Copilot.
    - 7 new tests covering strict-mode read-failure propagation, strict-mode soft-skip of per-line JSON corruption, `SessionTurnsLoadError` field round-trip, non-UUID-shape rejection, and the lexicographic top-advice ordering.
  - **Post-review hardening (H1–H3 from PR review)**:
    - **H1**: `loadSessionTurnsBySessionId` now distinguishes "not found / oversized" (returns `null` → 404) from "found but read/parse failed" (throws new exported `SessionTurnsLoadError` → 500). Previously the cache factory's `try { ... } catch { return [] }` swallowed real parse failures as empty results, which the diagnosis route then served as a green "looks healthy" panel — the worst-case failure mode for a quality-diagnosis tool. The single-session diagnosis path no longer routes through `FileCache.getOrCompute` (single-session lookup, infrequent, not a hot path); the sweep path's swallow is preserved unchanged.
    - **H2**: `computeSessionQuality` calls in both `readJsonlSession` and `appendSessionTail` are now wrapped in fail-soft `try/catch`. A throw in a future detector would have aborted the entire INSERT/UPDATE, leaving `byte_offset` stuck and the file re-throwing on every subsequent sweep. On detector failure we now log via `console.error` and persist neutral flags (`hasCompactionLoop=0`, `hasToolFailureStreak=0`, `maxContextFill=null`) — same shape the file-parse path already used. Tail path also gets the matching `PROFILE` fence.
    - **H3**: `DiagnosisPanel` fetch error handling rewritten. 5xx responses with non-JSON bodies (Next.js dev overlay, proxy 502) now surface status text instead of swallowing the body shape. `TypeError` (Chromium's "Failed to fetch") now renders as "Could not reach the server (is the dev server running?)" rather than the unhelpful default. Full error logged to `console.error` for the developer surface.
- **Wave 2.2 — CLAUDE.md health audit + @import resolution + context budget + memory editor.** Cluster D of the work-back plan in `~/.claude/plans/our-to-do-list-has-gentle-cookie.md`. The plan's "memory browser" sub-task (#193) was scoped down because the read path already shipped during the auto-memory work; this session adds the editor + stale warning on top of the existing route rather than migrating to a new path. Decision logged in plan note.
  - **`expandImports` helper** (`src/lib/scanner/expandImports.ts`). Recursive `@import <path>` resolution up to depth 5 with circular-import detection (visited Set keyed by `path.resolve`-canonicalized absolute paths), HTML block-comment stripping (Claude Code drops `<!-- ... -->` at load time), tilde expansion (`~/...` → home dir), and fenced-code-block awareness so doc examples like `` `@import ./foo.md` `` inside ``` blocks are left alone. Optional `preread` parameter lets callers that have already read the entry file pass its content in to avoid double-reads. Soft-fails on unreadable imports (records the error in the result, leaves the directive line verbatim, never throws).
  - **`auditClaudeMd` scanner** (`src/lib/scanner/claudeMdAudit.ts`). 0–100 health score implementing TODO #118's penalty formula: visibility cap (Claude Code truncates at 200 lines), file-size cap (>25 KB), inline-bloat detection (sections with >5 non-empty lines), missing-topic-files (>50-line index with no `@import` and no sibling `.md`), rules volume (`.claude/rules/**.md` total >2000 lines), and reference-tiering (rules files matching reference/guide/template/api/schema patterns >50 lines). Findings carry P0/P1/P2 severity, a one-line fix, and a per-finding penalty; severity-sorted on output. User-scope `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md` is read once per scan and cached in a module-scoped `Map` keyed by mtime so a parallel scan of 60 projects doesn't repeat the recursive `@import` expansion 60 times. Wired into `scanner/index.ts` so every project carries `claudeMdAudit?: ClaudeMdAuditInfo` after scan.
  - **`computeContextBudget`** (`src/lib/scanner/contextBudget.ts`). Component-model token estimator per TODO #135: 10 400 system base + (MCP servers × 400) + (skills in scope × 80) + (memory chars ÷ 4). MCP servers come from `scanMcpServers` (project + local + user + plugin + desktop + managed). Skills in scope = catalog's user + plugin + this-project's project-local entries. Memory bytes count post-`@import`-expanded `CLAUDE.md`, user-scope `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md`, and `.claude/rules/**.md` trees. USD estimate uses the input-token rate from `costCalculator` (default model `claude-sonnet-4-5`, `null` when pricing data is unavailable).
  - **`/api/projects/[slug]/context-budget` route**. Lazy: not part of the dashboard scan path. Hits the cached scan to resolve the project, then calls `computeContextBudget`. Each call recomputes from current MCP / skill / memory state — cheap because the catalog is cached in-memory.
  - **PATCH `/api/memory/[slug]`**. Adds write support to the existing memory route. Body: `{ file: string, content: string }`. New `memoryWriter.ts` module enforces: rejects path separators / null bytes (`TRAVERSAL`), `path.basename` strip, `.md`-only (`NOT_MARKDOWN`), final canonical-path containment check inside `<memoryDir>`. Filesystem writes go through a lazy `mkdir` + `writeFile` and surface errors as `WRITE_FAILED`. The dashboard refetches the file list after a successful save so mtime-driven UI signals (incl. the new stale badge) update immediately.
  - **`MemoryTab` editor + 30-day stale warning** (`src/components/MemoryTab.tsx`). New `MemoryEditorToolbar` switches the right-pane viewer between read mode (`MarkdownContent`) and edit mode (textarea + Save/Cancel). Save state surfaces as inline `Saving…` / `Saved` / `error code` text. File list rows now show a small uppercase `STALE` badge when `mtime` is ≥ 30 days old, with a tooltip naming the day count.
  - **`ClaudeMdAuditPanel` + `ContextBudgetPanel` + `ClaudeMdHealthBadge`** (`src/components/ClaudeMdAuditPanel.tsx`, `src/components/ContextBudgetPanel.tsx`). Audit panel renders the score chip (color-coded from green ≥80 → blue 60–79 → amber 40–59 → red <40), a one-line summary of total/visible lines / @imports / KB / rules counts, and findings grouped P0 → P1 → P2 with penalty deltas. Budget panel is collapsible (lazy-loads on first expand) and shows the four-row breakdown plus total tokens and USD. ProjectCard now shows a `ctx <score>` chip whenever the project's score drops below 80, alongside the existing todos / steps / insights chips.
  - **`ProjectDetail.Context` tab** now hosts (1) the audit panel, (2) the budget panel, and (3) the existing CLAUDE.md preview — in that order. The "no CLAUDE.md found" placeholder is now driven by `claudeMdAudit.hasClaudeMd` so it suppresses correctly when only the preview is missing but a CLAUDE.md exists.
  - **Help docs** — new `docs/help/claude-md-audit.md` (+ runtime copy at `public/help/`) explaining the formula, color thresholds, and limitations. `memory.md` extended with editor + stale-warning sections. `tabHelpMapping.context` retargeted to the new audit doc; `helpSlugs` extended; `HelpPanel` gets the new title.
  - **Scope-down note (vs plan §5.1.2)** — the plan called for a new `claudeMemory.ts` scanner and a route migration to `/api/projects/[slug]/memory`. Existing `scanner/memory.ts` + `/api/memory/[slug]` GET already covered the read path (auto-memory ships pre-Wave-2.2), so this session added PATCH on the existing route and a small writer module rather than churning the read path. Canonical-route migration is a follow-up if a future wave needs it.
  - **Tests** — 9 cases in `tests/expandImports.test.ts` (no-imports passthrough, single import inlining, full depth-5 recursion, depth-5 truncation flagged, circular-import non-recursion, HTML comment stripping, tilde expansion, fenced-code-block skip, soft-fail on missing import); 11 cases in `tests/claudeMdAudit.test.ts` (no-CLAUDE.md, perfect-score happy path, visibility-cap math, file-size penalty, inline-bloat detection, missing-topic-files trigger + suppression by `@import` presence, rules-volume + reference-tiering with `mockImplementation`-based path matching, score clamping, severity sort); 6 cases in `tests/contextBudget.test.ts` (system-base only, +400/MCP server, skills-by-source, memory-tokens math, USD estimation, end-to-end sum); 8 cases in `tests/memoryWriter.test.ts` (valid write, traversal via slash + backslash + null byte, non-md rejection, empty filename, lazy mkdir, FS error surface). 772 tests pass (1 skipped), typecheck clean.
- **Wave 2.1 — FTS5 session search + slug + continuation tracking.** Cluster C of the work-back plan in `~/.claude/plans/our-to-do-list-has-gentle-cookie.md`. Two of the four sub-tasks (#144 sub-task — restore `searchableText` under DB path; #146 — populate `sessions.status` at ingest) shipped during the P2c arc and required no new work; verified via the existing parity test (`tests/dataSessionsList.test.ts:255,263-270`). The other two land here.
  - **`/api/sessions/search?q=&scope=titles|prompts|both&limit=N` route** (`src/app/api/sessions/search/route.ts`). Backed by `prompts_fts` (FTS5) for body matches and `LIKE` over `sessions.{slug,initial_prompt,last_prompt,project_dir_name,git_branch}` for title-class matches. The `both` scope unions the two paths and dedups by `session_id` in JS, picking the higher score. Query input is FTS5-escaped via `buildFtsQuery` (per-token double-quoted with prefix wildcard) so user input containing `:` `"` `*` `(` etc. doesn't break the parser. Empty / sub-2-char `q` returns 400; FTS5 parse failure surfaces as `SessionSearchError` → 400 instead of letting the better-sqlite3 stack escape as 500. The route bypasses the v3-readiness gate intentionally — search reads `session_id` only, not cost columns.
  - **bm25 aggregation workaround** (`src/lib/data/sessionSearch.ts`). FTS5's `bm25()` function only works in row-context of a `MATCH` query; wrapping it in `MIN()` throws "unable to use function bm25 in the requested context". The query reads the `rank` virtual column (which equals bm25 by default) inside an inner subquery and aggregates `MIN(rank)` in the outer query — same result, no aggregation context error.
  - **SessionsBrowser debounced search** (`src/components/SessionsBrowser.tsx`). A 250ms-debounced fetch fires when search input has ≥2 chars, populating a `Set<sessionId>` of FTS5 hits. The client-side filter then `OR`s those hits with the existing title-class matches against the cached `searchableText` — so deep body matches that exceed the 4000-char preview cap surface, but title-class matches on un-indexed sessions still work. When the route returns `backend: "file"` (`MINDER_USE_DB=0`) the hit set stays empty and the filter is purely client-side. A small "FTS" badge on the search input makes the active backend visible — no silent fallback. Slug now also matches client-side.
  - **Schema v5: `sessions.slug` + `sessions.continued_from_session_id`** (`src/lib/db/migrations.ts`, `src/lib/db/schema.sql`). Idempotent ALTER pattern (matches v3): both columns nullable so legacy rows stay loadable until next ingest fills them. New `sessions_by_slug` partial index on `WHERE slug IS NOT NULL` keeps the slug → session_id resolver O(log N).
  - **Slug capture at ingest** (`src/lib/db/ingest.ts`, `src/lib/scanner/claudeConversations.ts`). Claude Code stamps a top-level `slug` field on every assistant entry once it's assigned one (verified empirically against 50+ real session JSONLs). Both ingest paths capture the first non-empty slug seen during the parse. `appendSessionTail` uses `COALESCE(slug, @slug)` so a tail's new slug never overwrites an existing one — Claude Code doesn't change slugs mid-session, but defending against it costs nothing.
  - **Continuation linking via post-reconcile UPDATE** (`src/lib/db/ingest.ts:refreshContinuationLinks`). Per-session linking can't see the full graph (the prior session might not be ingested yet, or this session might be the prior for one not yet read). Instead, after every session has been written, one correlated UPDATE points each session's `continued_from_session_id` at the most-recent prior session sharing the same slug. Tie-break on `session_id` keeps the link deterministic when start_ts collides. The function is exported for tests; production calls it once per `reconcileAllSessions`.
  - **Slug → session_id resolver in the data façade** (`src/lib/data/index.ts:resolveSlugToSessionId`). `getSessionDetail` now accepts either a UUID or a slug — the regex `/^[0-9a-f]{8}-(?:[0-9a-f]{4}-){3}[0-9a-f]{12}$/i` distinguishes; non-UUID lookups go through a `WHERE slug = ?` query on the indexed `sessions_by_slug` partial index, returning the most-recent matching `session_id`. Lets `/sessions/<slug>` routes resolve as stable URLs without a route refactor.
  - **`SessionSummary.slug` + `continuedFromSessionId`** (`src/lib/types.ts`). Both optional. SessionsBrowser shows a small "continued" badge on rows whose `continuedFromSessionId` is populated; tooltip names the predecessor. File-parse path captures `slug` but intentionally leaves `continuedFromSessionId` undefined — linking by slug requires corpus-wide visibility, which the file-parse pipeline doesn't have. Documented divergence; degraded but never wrong under `MINDER_USE_DB=0`.
  - **Tests** — 9 new cases across `tests/dbIngest.test.ts` (3 status snapshot scenarios + 1 slug capture + 2 continuation linking, including the negative case where two sessions in the same project but with different slugs do NOT link), and a full new file `tests/sessionSearch.test.ts` (7 cases covering FTS5 escaping, prompts/titles/both scope behavior, dedup, limit, invalid scope rejection). Migration-test counts bumped to v5. 733 tests pass, typecheck clean.
- **Wave 1.2 — COW config-history backups + ensureSchemaReady TTL refinement.** Second slice of the work-back plan in `~/.claude/plans/our-to-do-list-has-gentle-cookie.md` (Cluster B, partial — task #24 deferred, see plan §10.8).
  - **`configHistory` module** (`src/lib/configHistory.ts`) — `recordPreWrite(targetPath, opts?)`, `restore(backupId)`, `list({projectSlug?})`, `prune(now?)`. Snapshots write to `~/.minder/config-history/<id>/<basename>` (base64-encoded bytes), manifest at `~/.minder/config-history/manifest.jsonl`. BackupId format `<iso-ts>_<sha8|"missing">_<rand4>` (random suffix added in the PR-#59 review-fix commit; pre-fix format `<iso-ts>_<sha8>` could collide on same-ms same-content recordings). Each `recordPreWrite` records a fresh entry — no dedup-on-write; the smart-retention prune drops duplicates over time. `recordPreWrite` is fail-open: a snapshot failure logs a warning and returns null but never blocks the apply (a missing backup is unfortunate, an aborted apply is worse). Smart-retention `prune()` per TODO #56: every entry within 24h, daily for 7d, weekly for 30d, drop older. Auto-prune triggered opportunistically from `recordPreWrite` when last-prune timestamp (sidecar `.last-prune` file) is > 1h old.
  - **Apply-layer wiring** (`src/lib/template/apply.ts`) — every dispatch helper that writes a single file (agent, standalone skill, command, hook, MCP, workflow, settings-key, plugin enable) calls `snapshotBeforeApply()` with the target file path before invoking the primitive. Bundled-skill applies (which write a directory tree) intentionally pass through unwrapped — directory snapshots are a separate retention problem and out of Wave 1.2 scope. Dry-run applies never record. Snapshot label is `apply-<unitKind>:<unitKey>` so the Config History tab can show what triggered each entry.
  - **Config History tab** on `ProjectDetail` — `TabKey` union extended with `"config-history"`. Tab appears only when `/api/config-history?project=<slug>` returns at least one entry (lazily fetched on mount). `<ConfigHistoryTab>` component lists timestamp / target path / label / SHA-prefix / restore button per entry; restore round-trips through `POST /api/config-history/restore` and refreshes the list. `useToast` for success/failure. New help doc `docs/help/config-history.md` (+ runtime copy) describes the snapshot scope and retention policy.
  - **API routes** — `GET /api/config-history?project=<slug>` returns the manifest entries (filtered by project), `POST /api/config-history/restore` validates the BackupId via `list()` before calling `restore()` so a bad ID surfaces 404 rather than 500. Restore invalidates scan cache, claude-config route cache, and userConfigCache so the dashboard reflects the rolled-back file immediately.
  - **`ensureSchemaReady` 30s failure-TTL** (`src/lib/data/index.ts`) — replaces P2c's "clear cache on every failure" with a uniform 30s TTL on cached failures. P2c fixed the original bug (cached forever was poisoning every subsequent read) but introduced a new one: every dashboard poll re-ran `initDb()` end-to-end during a real outage, hammering the DB layer. The new contract: successful inits cache as before; failed inits cache for 30s before the next caller is allowed to re-attempt. In-flight callers still share the same promise. **Departure from plan §5.1.2 documented inline** — the plan's "cache forever for corrupt + 30s TTL" is internally inconsistent; picked the simpler uniform 30s policy because corruption can be repaired externally (operator deletes index.db) and we want to notice on the next retry. `tests/dataInitRetry.test.ts` first case rewritten to pin the new contract: cache held within 30s (initDb 1×) → fake-timer advance past TTL → cache expires (initDb 2×).
  - **Tests** — `tests/configHistory.test.ts` (15 cases) covers fail-open behavior, snapshot/restore round-trip, wasMissing semantics, project-slug filtering, malformed-line tolerance, restore-as-recorded-event semantics, and the smart-retention prune algorithm (24h kept whole, daily collapse in week, week collapse in month, drop > 30d). 682 tests pass, typecheck clean.
  - **DEFERRED: `~/.claude/mcp.json` merge** (plan task #24, original §5.1.2 third bullet). Surfaced during implementation that Claude Code's official docs (https://code.claude.com/docs/en/mcp) state user-scope MCP servers live in `~/.claude.json` (home-directory root, not under `.claude/`) — neither the plan's `~/.claude/mcp.json` nor Project Minder's existing `~/.claude/settings.json` read path matches Claude Code's actual storage. Skipped #24 to avoid layering a third incorrect source on top of two already-wrong ones. Follow-up TODO logged that scopes the broader audit (where IS user-scope MCP today, what's the precedence, does applyMcp's user-target need updating). Plan §10.8 carries the full context. **Resolved by Wave 1.2 follow-up below — multi-source MCP read.**
- **Wave 1.2 follow-up — multi-source MCP read.** Resolves the deferred mcp.json merge above by surfacing every canonical Claude Code (and Claude Desktop) MCP storage location, matching Claude Code's actual storage table at https://code.claude.com/docs/en/mcp.
  - **`McpSource` widened** (`src/lib/types.ts`) from `"project" | "user"` to `"project" | "user" | "local" | "plugin" | "desktop" | "managed"`. Only `"user"` and `"project"` are write targets via the apply layer; the four new sources are READ-ONLY in Project Minder.
  - **`applyMcp` rejects read-only sources** (`src/lib/template/applyMcp.ts`) with typed error `UNSUPPORTED_MCP_SOURCE_FOR_APPLY` so a misuse fails loudly at the closest sensible boundary instead of quietly promoting (e.g.) a Desktop-scoped server into a project's `.mcp.json`.
  - **`~/.claude.json` reader** (`src/lib/scanner/claudeJsonMcp.ts`) extracts ONLY `mcpServers` (user scope) and `projects[<path>].mcpServers` (local scope). Critical security boundary: this file contains OAuth tokens, telemetry IDs, and runtime state — the parsed root MUST NOT escape. Test (`tests/claudeJsonMcp.test.ts`) pins this with a fixture that includes OAuth-shaped strings and asserts none appear in the serialized output.
  - **Plugin-bundled MCP reader** (`src/lib/scanner/pluginMcp.ts`) walks each installed plugin's install path and reads `<installPath>/.mcp.json`. Per Claude Code's plugin spec, plugin manifests at `.claude-plugin/plugin.json` hold metadata only — no inline `mcpServers` — so we don't read that file for MCP entries.
  - **Claude Desktop config reader** (`src/lib/scanner/desktopMcp.ts`) reads `~/Library/Application Support/Claude/claude_desktop_config.json` (macOS) or `%APPDATA%\Claude\claude_desktop_config.json` (Windows). Linux returns `[]` — no published Desktop client.
  - **Managed MCP reader** (`src/lib/scanner/managedMcp.ts`) reads the system-level admin-deployed `managed-mcp.json` (macOS `/Library/Application Support/ClaudeCode/`, Linux/WSL `/etc/claude-code/`, Windows `C:\Program Files\ClaudeCode\`). Fails open silently on ENOENT/EACCES — these are the *expected* states on machines without admin policy, so we deliberately suppress them.
  - **`getUserConfig()` merges all sources** (`src/lib/userConfigCache.ts`). All five reads (settings.json + claude.json + plugin + desktop + managed) run in parallel via `Promise.all`. The merge order surfaces the source-precedence story: managed → user-from-settings.json → user-from-claude.json → desktop → plugin. No dedup on name collisions across sources — both entries surface and the apply policy + UI grouping decide what to do. Local-scope per-project servers are surfaced separately (via `readLocalScopeMcpFromClaudeJson(projectPath)`) and don't leak into the global "user" list.
  - **Tests** — 18 new test cases across `tests/claudeJsonMcp.test.ts` (OAuth-leak prevention, env-value stripping, per-project mapping, convenience-wrapper round-trips) and the `applyMcp` rejection-guard suite (4 read-only sources × refuse-with-typed-error + sanity that user/project still apply). 696 tests pass, typecheck clean.
- **Wave 1.2 — review-feedback fixes (PR #59 follow-up).** Resolves 11 review comments from Copilot + Codex on PR #59 across the Wave 1.2 work.
  - **P1 — `BackupId` collision-resistant** (`src/lib/configHistory.ts`). Old format `<iso-ts>_<sha8|missing>` could collide for two snapshots in the same millisecond on identical bytes (or any two missing-file snapshots), causing ambiguous restore, React key collisions, and snapshot path aliasing. New format `<iso-ts>_<sha8|missing>_<rand4>` adds 32 bits of randomness — collision probability is negligible. New test case fires 20 concurrent `recordPreWrite` calls on identical bytes and asserts all 20 ids are distinct.
  - **P1 — Snapshot rollback for no-op applies** (`src/lib/template/apply.ts`). `snapshotBeforeApply` ran before the apply primitive decided whether to write. With `conflict: "skip"` (and similar no-op paths), the manifest filled with misleading "restore points" for events that never touched disk. New `removeBackup(id)` API + `finalizeSnapshots(ids, result)` helper roll back the snapshot if the apply result is `skipped` / `would-apply` / `error`. Every dispatcher (agent / skill / command / hook / mcp / workflow / settings / plugin) routes through the new pattern: `const snaps = await snapshotBeforeApply(...); return finalizeSnapshots(snaps, await applyXxx(...));`.
  - **P1 — Prune read-modify-write under one lock** (`src/lib/configHistory.ts`). `prune()` previously read the manifest via `list()`, computed its retention decision, then re-acquired `withFileLock` to rewrite — a concurrent `recordPreWrite` append landing between read and rewrite was silently dropped. The full read+decide+write cycle now lives inside a single `withFileLock` scope.
  - **P2 — Byte-faithful restore** (`src/lib/configHistory.ts` + `src/lib/atomicWrite.ts`). `restore()` decoded the base64 snapshot to a Buffer then converted it to UTF-8 text before writing — corrupting any non-UTF-8 / binary content. `writeFileAtomic` extended to accept `string | Buffer` (raw bytes when given a Buffer, no transcoding); `restore()` now passes the decoded Buffer through unchanged. New test pins this with a fixture containing invalid-UTF-8 bytes (lone surrogates, raw 0xFF, PNG header) and asserts bit-exact equality after restore.
  - **P2 — Catalog + commands cache invalidation on restore** (`src/app/api/config-history/restore/route.ts`). Restore can target agent / skill / command / workflow files but the route only cleared scan/config caches — those views stayed stale until TTL. Added `invalidateCatalogCache()` + `invalidateCommandsRouteCache()` to mirror the apply path's invalidation set.
  - **P2 — Preserve project slug for `target.kind === "path"`** (`src/lib/template/apply.ts`). Template applies to newly-bootstrapped projects route through the `path` branch (post-bootstrap), so their snapshots had `projectSlug: undefined` and were excluded from `/api/config-history?project=<slug>`. New `resolveProjectSlugForSnapshot()` helper looks up the slug from the cached scan when target is path-kind. Returns `undefined` for paths that don't match a scanned project — those still record under the global manifest, just unscoped.
  - **P2 — Strip server-local `snapshotPath` from `/api/config-history` GET response** (`src/app/api/config-history/route.ts`). The browser doesn't need a path inside `~/.minder/config-history/`; surfacing it just couples the client to filesystem layout. New test (`tests/configHistoryApi.test.ts`) pins the stripping with a string match against `.minder/config-history` in the serialized response.
  - **P2 — Wrap `list()` in try/catch in restore route** (`src/app/api/config-history/restore/route.ts`). Manifest I/O errors (permissions, FS corruption) escaped as opaque crashes; now surface as structured 500 JSON.
  - **P2 — Fix `shortTs()` for restore toast** (`src/components/ConfigHistoryTab.tsx`). Function received the `BackupId` after restore and tried to reverse its `:` → `-` substitution — the regex didn't account for the format's trailing suffix, so toasts often showed the raw id. Now the caller passes the entry's `timestamp` (always ISO) directly; the function simplified to drop the dead id-handling branch.
  - **P2 — Per-flag saving state in Settings** (`src/components/SettingsPage.tsx`). `useState<FeatureFlagKey | null>` raced under overlapping toggles: the second toggle's `setSaving(b)` clobbered the first; the first toggle's `setSaving(null)` on completion cleared the second's indicator. Now a `ReadonlySet<FeatureFlagKey>` tracks every in-flight key independently.
  - **Tests** — 9 new test cases across `tests/configHistory.test.ts` (BackupId uniqueness, byte-faithful binary restore, `removeBackup` round-trip + no-op-on-unknown semantics) and new `tests/configHistoryApi.test.ts` (snapshotPath stripped from response, project filter passthrough, ENOENT empty-list 200). 706 tests pass, typecheck clean.
- **Wave 1.2 — second-round review fixes (PR #59 follow-up).** Resolves 7 additional review comments from Copilot + Codex on PR #59 after the first fix-pass.
  - **P1 — `dispatchMcp` source-aware lookup** (`src/lib/template/apply.ts`). The user-scope merged list now includes managed/desktop/plugin entries alongside actual user-scope ones. `findMcpByKey` matches by name only — without a writable-source filter, a managed/desktop/plugin server sharing a name with a user-scope one would win the lookup (managed-first merge order made that the typical outcome) and `applyMcp` would then reject with `UNSUPPORTED_MCP_SOURCE_FOR_APPLY`. Surfaced as "can't apply" even when a writable user-scope entry existed. Filter `s.source === "user"` before lookup keeps the resolution honest. Test (`tests/applyDispatch.test.ts`) pins this with a fixture where a `desktop`-source shadow precedes the writable `user`-source entry in merge order.
  - **P2 — Local-scope `~/.claude.json` MCP wired into project scans** (`src/lib/scanner/mcpServers.ts`). Pre-fix, `readClaudeJsonMcp.byProject` was parsed but never propagated — local-scope per-project servers were invisible. `scanMcpServers(projectPath)` now merges its project `.mcp.json` entries with `readLocalScopeMcpFromClaudeJson(projectPath)` so per-project MCP visibility matches what Claude Code itself sees. New per-process cache in `claudeJsonMcp.ts` (5s TTL on `globalThis`) prevents an N-project scan burst from re-parsing `~/.claude.json` once per project. Test (`tests/mcpServers.test.ts`) pins the merged shape with path-aware fs mocking.
  - **P2 — Single `loadInstalledPlugins()` walk in `getUserConfig`** (`src/lib/userConfigCache.ts`). Pre-fix, `readPluginScopeMcp()` (in the parallel block) and `readPluginsInfo()` each walked the plugin registry — doubling N file reads per cache refresh (`installed_plugins.json` plus each plugin's `.claude-plugin/plugin.json` for repo URL extraction). `readUserConfig` now loads plugins once and threads the result through both consumers via optional parameters (`readPluginScopeMcp(installed?)` and `readPluginsInfo(claudeDir, settings, prefetchedInstalled?)`). Standalone callers without the prefetch still work — defaults to a self-contained walk.
  - **P2 — Fake-timer leak in `tests/dataInitRetry.test.ts`** wrapped in try/finally so `vi.useRealTimers()` runs even when an assertion throws — prevents fake timers from poisoning later tests in the same file.
  - **Docs alignment** — `HistoryEntry.id` docstring and the Wave 1.2 changelog bullet updated to reflect the actual BackupId format `<iso-ts>_<sha8|"missing">_<rand4>` (the random suffix was added in the first review-fix commit but the docstrings still described the pre-fix `<iso-ts>_<sha8>` format and a non-existent dedup-by-hash behavior). `McpSource` docstring updated to remove the inaccurate "or inline in `<plugin-root>/plugin.json`" claim — Claude Code's plugin spec defines `plugin.json` as metadata-only, and `readPluginScopeMcp` reads only `.mcp.json`.
  - **Tests** — 2 new cases (filter-merged-list-by-writable-source in `tests/applyDispatch.test.ts`, local-scope merge in `tests/mcpServers.test.ts`). 708 tests pass, typecheck clean.
- **Wave 1.2 — third-round review fixes (PR #59 follow-up).** Resolves 3 additional Codex P2 comments on PR #59 after the second fix-pass.
  - **Reentrant `withFileLock` + snapshot under same lock** (`src/lib/atomicWrite.ts` + `src/lib/template/apply.ts`). Pre-fix the snapshot was recorded BEFORE the apply primitive acquired its target-file lock — two concurrent applies on the same file could both snapshot the same pre-write bytes (because both reads happened before either lock acquired), so restoring the second backup would revert past both operations and break one-step rollback semantics. `withFileLock` is now reentrant via `AsyncLocalStorage`: tracks which paths the current async context already holds, skips the FIFO queue on re-acquisition. Each apply dispatcher now wraps its `snapshotBeforeApply` + `applyXxx` pair in `withFileLock(targetFile, ...)`; the apply primitive's internal `withFileLock(targetFile, ...)` runs as a no-op because the dispatcher already holds it. Cross-chain serialization unchanged. New test file (`tests/fileLockReentrant.test.ts`, 5 cases) pins reentrancy + cross-chain mutex + cross-path concurrency + visibility semantics.
  - **Slug fallback for fresh-bootstrap path targets** (`src/lib/template/apply.ts`). `applyTemplate` routes new-project bootstraps through `target.kind === "path"` and applies units BEFORE refreshing the scan cache, so `resolveProjectSlugForSnapshot`'s scan lookup missed and backups were recorded with no projectSlug — excluded from `/api/config-history?project=<slug>`. Added a fallback that derives the slug from `path.basename(target.path)` via the same `toLowerCase + kebab` transform the scanner uses, so the entry surfaces in the project's Config History tab as soon as the post-bootstrap scan picks the project up.
  - **Project-source MCP apply lookup filters out local-scope shadows** (`src/lib/template/apply.ts`). Mirrors the user-source filter from the previous round: `scanMcpServers` now merges project-scope (`.mcp.json`) with local-scope (`~/.claude.json` `projects[<path>].mcpServers`) entries, both arriving in the project-source dispatch branch. Without filtering, `findMcpByKey` could resolve to a `local`-source entry and `applyMcp` would deterministically reject with `UNSUPPORTED_MCP_SOURCE_FOR_APPLY`. Now filters to `s.source === "project"` before lookup.
  - **Tests** — 7 new cases across `tests/fileLockReentrant.test.ts` (5 cases pinning reentrancy semantics), `tests/applyDispatch.test.ts` (project-source filter parallel to the user-source filter), and `tests/configHistory.test.ts` (recordPreWrite slug-passthrough contract). 715 tests pass, typecheck clean.
- **Wave 1.2 — fourth-round review fixes (PR #59 follow-up).** Resolves 2 final Codex comments on PR #59 — 1 P1 + 1 P2.
  - **P1 — `dispatchMcp` ambiguity guard for cross-file user-scope name collisions** (`src/lib/template/apply.ts`). The writable-source filter (`s.source === "user"`) still let through entries from BOTH `~/.claude/settings.json` AND `~/.claude.json` (both tagged `source: "user"` by `parseMcpServers`). `findMcpByKey` matches by name only — silently picking the first by merge order would apply the WRONG entry's command/env. Added an ambiguity guard: when more than one writable-source entry shares a name, return typed error `AMBIGUOUS_MCP_SOURCE` listing both source files so the user is forced to deduplicate rather than getting silently-wrong behavior.
  - **P2 — `restore` mutation under `withFileLock(targetPath)`** (`src/lib/configHistory.ts`). Pre-fix `restore` mutated `entry.targetPath` (delete or write) without acquiring `withFileLock`. A concurrent apply on the same file could race the restore's write — the lock the apply dispatcher holds doesn't help if the restore path doesn't take the same lock. Now wraps the entire snapshot+mutate sequence in `withFileLock(entry.targetPath, ...)`. Reentrant lock means inner `recordPreWrite`/`writeFileAtomic` paths share the held lock without deadlock.
  - **Tests** — 2 new cases: `tests/applyDispatch.test.ts` pins the `AMBIGUOUS_MCP_SOURCE` typed error with both source paths in the message; `tests/configHistory.test.ts` pins restore's lock acquisition by serializing it behind an outer `withFileLock` holder and asserting event ordering. 717 tests pass, typecheck clean.
- **Wave 1.1 — Settings page, feature flags, AppNav sub-menu refactor.** Foundation slice for the work-back plan in `~/.claude/plans/our-to-do-list-has-gentle-cookie.md`. Three pieces ship together because every later wave depends on at least one of them.
  - **`/settings` page** (`src/app/settings/page.tsx` + `src/components/SettingsPage.tsx`) with a left-rail nav and 8 sections (Features, Appearance, Cost, Notifications, Integrations, Data & Privacy, Terminal, Auto-title). Wave 1 ships the **Features** section in full; the other 7 render a "Coming in wave N" placeholder so the IA is final on day one.
  - **`featureFlags` module** (`src/lib/featureFlags.ts`) with a typed `FeatureFlagKey` union, `getFlag()` accessor (defaults to ON), `isFeatureFlagKey()` validator, and `FEATURE_FLAG_META[]` for the Settings UI. 12 flags defined: `scanInsights`, `scanTodos`, `scanManualSteps`, `scanClaudeSessions`, `scanWorktrees`, `scanDockerCompose`, `manualStepsWatcher`, `gitStatusCache`, `usageAnalytics`, `agentSkillIndexer`, `devServerControl`, `liveActivity`. Six are **wired today** (the scanner-orchestrator gates); six persist for later waves and surface a "not wired" hint in the UI so users know the toggle doesn't yet move anything.
  - **Scanner orchestrator gating** (`src/lib/scanner/index.ts`) — `scanProject()` consults the flags map once per scan and substitutes neutral values for disabled scanners (`EMPTY_DOCKER`, `EMPTY_CLAUDE_SESSIONS`, `undefined` for the optional `?:` fields). Downstream code (`lastActivity` derivation, `ProjectCard`) sees the same shape it always did. Worktree overlay attachment is gated at the orchestrator level so disabling worktree scan also stops the overlay walk.
  - **`gitStatusCache.dispose()` and `manualStepsWatcher.dispose()`** added for the future hot-toggle path. Today no UI calls them; the Settings copy tells the user a server restart is required for active-subsystem flag changes.
  - **`PATCH /api/config` extension** — accepts `featureFlags: Partial<Record<FeatureFlagKey, boolean>>` with strict validation: unknown keys reject the whole patch (no silent merge — matches the established no-silent-fallbacks posture from P2b-9), non-boolean values reject the whole patch. Partial-merge semantics: caller sends only the flags they want to change.
  - **AppNav refactor** (`src/components/AppNav.tsx`) — collapses 11 top-level links into Projects (root) + 3 dropdowns (Catalog: Agents/Skills/Commands/Plugins/Templates · Sessions: Sessions/Plans/Stats/Usage/SQL · Config: Hooks/MCP/Settings/Setup/Status/Insights/Steps) + a gear icon to `/settings`. Hooks/MCP entries deep-link to `/config?type=hooks|mcp` (no new routes); active-state computation reads pathname AND the `?type=` query so the right child highlights inside the dropdown. Dropdown trigger shows a small `•` indicator when any child carries a non-zero pulse badge. `useSearchParams()` use forces a `Suspense` boundary in the layout — added.
  - **Placeholder pages** for `/plans`, `/plugins`, `/sql` so the new nav links don't 404 before Wave 5 lands. Each page reuses a shared `<ComingSoonPage />` component that names the wave, cluster, and TODO refs.
  - **`MinderConfig` extended** with `featureFlags`, `currency`, `scheduleMode`, `terminal`, `telegram`, `pricingRules` — all optional; `DEFAULT_CONFIG` unchanged so existing `.minder.json` files load with zero migration. `PricingRule` and `ScheduleMode` types added as placeholders that later waves (Cluster S, Wave 8) will tighten.
  - **Help docs** — `docs/help/settings.md` (+ `public/help/settings.md` runtime copy) describe the section roster and the per-flag wiring posture; `src/lib/help-mapping.ts` wires `/settings → settings`.
  - **Tests** — `tests/featureFlags.test.ts` (16 cases) covers default-on semantics, partial-config behavior, the `false-vs-undefined` regression guard (`|| defaultOn` would flip `false` → `true`; `?? defaultOn` is safe), key uniqueness, group partition completeness, and the `isFeatureFlagKey` validator. 656 tests pass, typecheck clean.

### Changed
- **Enforce the `postcss` version floor under pnpm (issue #179).** The `postcss: ">=8.5.10"` floor lived only in the top-level npm `overrides` block, which pnpm ignores — so it never constrained resolution, and `next@16.2.6` quietly bundled `postcss@8.4.31`. Now that the repo is pnpm-only (#164), the dead top-level `overrides` block is removed entirely and the dependency floors are consolidated into `pnpm-workspace.yaml`'s `overrides` (alongside the existing `onlyBuiltDependencies`), rather than `package.json`'s `pnpm.overrides`: pnpm 11+ no longer reads the `pnpm` field of `package.json`, so keeping overrides there would silently drop the floor for any contributor on pnpm 11. The `postcss` range is `>=8.5.10 <9` — floored at the patched line and capped below the next major so a future breaking `postcss@9` can't satisfy it; `zod`'s `3.25.76` pin moves with it. `pnpm-lock.yaml` regenerated: the tree now resolves a single `postcss@8.5.15` (Next's bundled `8.4.31` forced up across the backward-compatible 8.x line). No known vulnerability was present (`8.4.31` already patched CVE-2023-44270); this makes the declared intent real rather than misrepresented. Verified with `pnpm build` + full suite.
- **Build tooling: complete the pnpm migration; CI no longer uses npm (issue #164).** The repo had been half-migrated — local dev used pnpm (`pnpm-lock.yaml`, `pnpm-workspace.yaml`, `pnpm.onlyBuiltDependencies`) while CI still ran `npm ci` against a stale `package-lock.json`. Since PR #159 pinned `zod` to `3.25.76` in `pnpm.overrides` (which the npm lockfile never reflected), `npm ci` failed on every PR with `Invalid: lock file's zod@4.3.6 does not satisfy zod@3.25.76`, forcing every merge through `--admin`. Changes: (1) `.github/workflows/{ci,release,pr-review-responder}.yml` now run `pnpm/action-setup@v4` before `actions/setup-node` (so `cache: 'pnpm'` can compute its key) and use `pnpm install --frozen-lockfile` + `pnpm <script>`; the global Claude Code CLI install in pr-review-responder stays on `npm install -g` since it's a global binary, not a project dep. (2) Deleted the stale `package-lock.json` — `pnpm-lock.yaml` is now the sole lockfile. (3) Added `"packageManager": "pnpm@10.30.3"` to `package.json` so `pnpm/action-setup` and `corepack` resolve the pinned version automatically. (4) Internal `package.json` scripts (`predev`, `prebuild`, `capture:docs:all`) switched from `npm run` to `pnpm`. (5) `scripts/setup-hooks.mjs` writes a pre-commit hook running `pnpm typecheck && pnpm test --pool=forks` (was npm); doc comments in `probe-otel.mjs`/`typecheck.mjs` updated. (6) `CLAUDE.md` Commands/Testing/Verification sections and `docs/help/{contributing,getting-started,mcp-server}.md` (+ `public/help/` mirrors) now reference pnpm. Note: this PR left the dead top-level npm `overrides` block in place — its `postcss` floor (`>=8.5.10`) was never actually enforced under pnpm (Next bundles `postcss@8.4.31`, which slips through because the floor lived only in npm `overrides`, not a pnpm-honored location); that dead-floor finding was filed separately rather than risk a postcss resolution change in a CI-fix PR, and is now resolved by #179 (see above).
- **Performance — P0 residual client wins.** Four targeted improvements closing out the originally-deferred P0 quick wins: (1) `MarkdownContent` wrapped in `React.memo` with parse loop hoisted to a `useMemo`-guarded `buildElements` helper — previously re-parsed on every parent render. (2) `ManualStepsNavBadge` drops its independent 30s `/api/manual-steps?pending=true` poller; reads `usePulse().snapshot.pendingSteps` instead (5s shared, paused when tab hidden). (3) `ManualStepsDashboard` outer project list virtualized via `@tanstack/react-virtual` with dynamic-height `measureElement`; Expand all / Collapse all toggle preserved. (4) `SparklineList` table converted to CSS grid + virtualized rows; per-row `pendingTodos`, `pendingSteps`, and `lastSession` computations hoisted to a memoized `enrichedSorted` array. No new deps.
- **Memory file browser — conflict-safe saves.** The project-detail Memory tab now performs optimistic-concurrency saves. The GET `?file=` response carries `mtimeMs`; the PATCH body accepts it back as an optional `expectedMtimeMs` field. If the file changed on disk between open and save, the server returns 409 MTIME_CONFLICT and the tab shows a toast with a **Reload** action to pull the latest content. A 2 MB size cap (413 TOO_LARGE) and pre-write config-history backup were also added to `writeMemoryFile`. Successful saves now surface a toast notification. Navigating away with an unsaved draft triggers a browser `beforeunload` confirmation.
- **Settings page** — "W7" / "W8" / "W10" developer-only wave badges replaced with "Soon" labels; placeholder sections now say "Coming soon." instead of "Coming in wave N."
- **Schedule page** — removed developer-only wave version reference from the coming-soon blurb.
- **Feature flag descriptions** — stripped internal wave references from the Settings UI labels for 6 flags: Usage analytics, Agent/skill indexer, Dev server control, Live activity, Task dispatcher, and MCP security scan.
- **Test infrastructure** — shared `UsageTurn` fixture builder extracted to `tests/usage/_fixtures.ts` (`makeTurn`, `assistant`, `user`, `readTurn`, `editTurn`, `mcpCallTurn`); four test files updated to import from it.
- **`DiagnosisPanel`** — removed stale local `formatUsd` and `HeaderStat` remnants; now fully uses `formatCost` from `@/lib/format` and `StatCell` from `ui/StatCell`.
- **Settings page** — "W7" / "W8" / "W10" developer-only wave badges replaced with "Soon" labels; placeholder sections now say "Coming soon." instead of "Coming in wave N."
- **Schedule page** — removed developer-only wave version reference from the coming-soon blurb.
- **Feature flag descriptions** — stripped internal wave references from the Settings UI labels for 6 flags: Usage analytics, Agent/skill indexer, Dev server control, Live activity, Task dispatcher, and MCP security scan.
- **Test infrastructure** — shared `UsageTurn` fixture builder extracted to `tests/usage/_fixtures.ts` (`makeTurn`, `assistant`, `user`, `readTurn`, `editTurn`, `mcpCallTurn`); four test files updated to import from it.
- **`DiagnosisPanel`** — removed stale local `formatUsd` and `HeaderStat` remnants; now fully uses `formatCost` from `@/lib/format` and `StatCell` from `ui/StatCell`.
- `GET /api/agent-view/stream` now starts both the daemon-roster watcher and the JSONL-creation watcher on first connect.
- `LiveAgentSession` gains `lastToolFailed?: boolean` — true when the session's most recent `PostToolUse` hook event carried a failure signal within the last 2 minutes.
- `GET /api/live-activity/install` now includes `lastReceivedAt: number | null` in its response.
- **Agent Observatory Wave 3 — Internal linking + freshness polish.** Four "free wins" that activate already-stubbed UI and connect Observatory to three sibling features it had never touched: (A) **Live cost + context fill** — `LiveAgentSession.costEstimate` and `maxContextFill` (declared in types, stubbed in UI since Wave 1) are now populated by a new `liveCostCache.ts` helper that wraps `parseSessionTurns` with a per-session mtime-keyed reduction cache so the aggregator can enrich on every SSE delta without re-parsing JSONL. All three aggregator paths (daemon, hook-only, JSONL fallback) call `getLiveSessionMetrics` in parallel via `Promise.all`; terminal sessions are skipped (their data lives in the historical session detail view). (B) **Freshness clock** — `AgentViewToolbar` now accepts a `lastEventAt` prop, ticks it with a 1-second interval, and renders "Updated Xs ago" next to the Live indicator; the chip turns amber after 30s of silence on a connected stream so users can distinguish quiet-but-healthy from stalled. (C) **Catalog cross-reference in the tree tab** — `/api/agent-view/tree` now decorates each `OrchNode` with catalog emoji, color, and description when the agent name matches an entry in the agents catalog (5-min TTL alias-map cache); `AgentTreeView` renders matched nodes as styled links to `/agents?q=<name>` and exposes an inline ⓘ description expand with no navigation required. (D) **Insights tab in the peek panel** — `AgentPeekPanel` gains a third tab "Insights" (keyboard-nav updated to 3 tabs); the peek route now reads insights directly from the session JSONL via `parseInsightsFromJsonl` (bypassing the lazily-synced INSIGHTS.md for freshness) with a mtime-keyed cache; a count badge on the tab header lights up as soon as the first `★ Insight` block is written. 13 new tests across `tests/liveCostCache.test.ts` (8) and `tests/aggregate_metrics.test.ts` (5). Roadmap for Waves 4-9 captured in `docs/brainstorming/agent-observatory-roadmap.md`.
- `LiveAgentSession.costEstimate` and `maxContextFill` are now populated for active (non-terminal) sessions in `aggregateLiveSessions`.
- `AgentViewToolbar` accepts a new optional `lastEventAt?: number | null` prop and self-ticks a freshness display with `setInterval(1000)`.
- `OrchNode` in `orchestrationGraph.ts` gains optional `catalogEmoji`, `catalogColor`, `catalogDescription` fields populated by the tree API route.
- **Agent Observatory Wave 2 — Sub-agent in-flight badge + lazy tree tab.** Extends the `/agent-view` Kanban with two new surfaces: (1) a `+N` chip in the `AgentCard` footer when one or more sub-agents are currently spawned but not yet stopped, derived from the hook buffer without any new tracker module (formula: `count(PreToolUse where toolName="Agent") − count(SubagentStop)` per sessionId, clamped to 0); (2) a tabbed "Sub-agents" tab in the `AgentPeekPanel` drawer backed by `AgentTreeView`, which lazily fetches `GET /api/agent-view/tree?sessionId=X` only when the tab is opened, calls `loadOrchestrationGraph(sessionId)` (the existing JSONL-replay path from `src/lib/usage/orchestrationGraph.ts`), and renders the parent→child tree with depth, status colour, and agent names. The tab header mirrors the in-flight badge count so users know to look before clicking. Pure-JSONL sessions (no hooks) have no badge and the tree shows post-hoc replay only. 7 new tests in `tests/agentView_subagents.test.ts` cover the badge formula edge cases: zero events, spawns-without-stops, decremented on stop, clamped to zero (stop-exceeds-spawn), and cross-session isolation.
- **Agent Observatory Wave 1 — Live Kanban at `/agent-view`.** Real-time operational view of all running Claude Code sessions across your projects. Merges three data sources in priority order: (1) the Claude daemon roster (`~/.claude/daemon/roster.json` + `~/.claude/jobs/*/state.json`) — same files Agent View reads, zero user setup for `claude --bg` sessions; (2) the existing hook event ring for sessions with Live Activity enabled; (3) JSONL tail inference as a fallback for all sessions. Six-column Kanban (Needs Input / Working / Idle / Completed / Failed / Stopped) mirrors Claude Agent View's state model but surfaces it in the browser with cross-project visibility, cost chips, context-fill warnings, and a Peek panel. The Peek panel is the first consumer of the previously dead-storage hook ring buffer (`getHookBuffer(slug)` in `src/lib/hooks/buffer.ts`), surfacing the last 30 hook events per session. SSE transport (`/api/agent-view/stream`) pushes snapshots on every JSONL append (via the ingest watcher bridge) and every hook event; 15 s heartbeat defeats proxy timeouts; auto-reconnect with 1s → 5s → 15s backoff, polling fallback after 2 failures. Abandoned-session reaper drops sessions silent for > 180 min (configurable via `.minder.json` `agentView.abandonThresholdMin`). New `agentView` feature flag (defaults on). New navigation entry in the Sessions group in the sidebar. Wave 2 (live parent→child sub-agent tree) is planned for the next wave.
- **Sidebar project-switcher glyph re-skinned to the amber brand mark "PM".** The 28×28 glyph at the top of the left sidebar (in `AppSidebar.tsx` — the button that opens the project-scope picker) previously used a blue→purple gradient (`var(--info)` → `var(--purple)`) and rendered the first letter of the selected scope (or "∞" when scope was `all`). That predated the amber-accent design system and read off-brand. The glyph now uses an amber gradient (`var(--accent)` → `var(--accent-strong)`) with a fixed "PM" mark, font-size dropped from 13px to 11px to fit two letters in the same 28×28 footprint, plus `letter-spacing: 0.02em` to keep the pair from feeling cramped. The active scope is still visible from `.scope-name` immediately to the right of the glyph — the glyph is now a constant brand affordance, not a scope indicator. `aria-hidden="true"` on the glyph since "PM" is a brand mark, not meaningful content; the button itself has an `aria-label="Project: {scope}. Click to switch project."` so screen readers always get the accessible name (closes Copilot PR #117 a11y finding). Removed the now-unused `scopeInitial` derived variable.
- **Phase 1 (#148) — Resilient `ensureSchemaReady()`.** The schema-readiness gate in `src/lib/data/index.ts` now classifies init failures and retries transient errors (EBUSY/EPERM/ENOENT/ENOTEMPTY/SQLITE_BUSY/SQLITE_LOCKED) up to 4 attempts with [100/300/900] ms backoff before caching. A single Windows EBUSY during ingest write contention no longer downgrades every dashboard read for the next 30 s. The state machine has 5 terminal/transition states (`idle | in-flight | success | transient-failed | permanent-failed`); `permanent-failed` is reached after two cumulative quarantine observations and is sticky until process exit. New `getInitStatus()` export surfaces the snapshot.
- **`renameWithRetry`** (`src/lib/atomicWrite.ts`) — extends retry-eligible code list to include `ENOTEMPTY` (Windows directory-handle release lag).
- **Phase 7 — Hygiene pass.** Touches many files; six of nine planned steps shipped. Verification: typecheck clean, **2030 tests passing** (1 skipped, +1 over Phase 6 for the prep golden vector). Atomic per-chunk commits so any future regression can be bisected.
  - **Step 5 — Fused `computeSessionQuality` walks.** Was: 4 separate turn-walks (max-fill, computeCacheStats, detectCompactionLoops, detectToolFailureStreaks). Now: one walk that builds the per-assistant fill projection, the tool-failure evaluable projection, the cache totals, and max-fill simultaneously. The two window-scan post-passes (`scanCompactionPairs`, `scanFailureWindows`) extracted to private helpers so per-detector exports delegate to the same code path. Pinned by a prep-commit golden vector — all 2030 tests pass byte-equal.
  - **Step 8 — `ClaudeMdAuditInfo` → discriminated union.** `{ hasClaudeMd: false, findings } | { hasClaudeMd: true, score, projectLines, importCount, fileBytes, rulesLines, rulesFileCount, findings }`. Consumers switch on the discriminant — TS narrows to the present variant inside the truthy branch so the `!` non-null assertions in `ProjectCard` and `ProjectDetail` are gone. `ProjectData.claudeMdAudit` is now required (the scanner always populates it).
  - **Steps 3+9 — Format helpers + typecheck wrapper.** Added `formatPct`, `formatDurationSeconds`, `formatDurationMs`, `formatDurationMsCompact`, `formatTokensOrDash` to `src/lib/format.ts` and replaced 9 files' worth of duplicate local helpers (`DiagnosisPanel`, `EfficiencyTab`, `SessionDetailView`, `StatsDashboard`, `ProjectSessions`, `SessionsBrowser`, `UsageDashboard`, `sessionDiagnosis.ts`). `SessionTimeline` keeps its local sub-second-precision variant intentionally. New `scripts/typecheck.mjs` purges `tsconfig.tsbuildinfo` before invoking `tsgo` so a stale incremental cache from a prior branch can't mask real errors; `npm run typecheck` (used by pre-commit + CI) goes through the wrapper.
  - **Step 6 — `resolveSessionJsonl` resolver.** Was: same `~/.claude/projects/<dir>/<sessionId>.jsonl` fs-walk fallback inlined in `parser.ts:findSessionFile`, two other parser.ts spots, and `claudeConversations.ts:scanSessionDetail`. Now: one shared resolver in `src/lib/usage/sessionPath.ts` with consistent UUID/hex validation + ENOENT handling.
  - **Step 4 — `tests/usage/fixtures/turn.ts`.** Shared `makeTurn` / `assistantTurn` / `userTurn` factories. Existing per-file `makeTurn` helpers in classifier/costCalculator/oneShotDetector were intentionally NOT refactored — each carries domain-specific defaults the existing assertions depend on; blanket refactor would change behavior. Fixture sits as canonical for new tests.
  - **Plan deviations** (recorded in plan's Risks section): (a) Format helpers consolidated into `src/lib/format.ts`, not `src/lib/utils.ts` — `formatTokens`/`formatCost` were already there per Phase 4's import; same path-wrong pattern as Phase 6's `config/schema.ts`. (b) Steps 1+2+7 (extract `FindingCard` / `StatCell` / `severityTokens`) **deferred to Phase 7.1** — the three finding-card call sites have meaningfully different field shapes (`DiagnosisFinding` vs `WasteFinding` vs `ClaudeMdAuditFinding`) and different severity taxonomies; honest extraction needs a richer props union than the plan implied, with visible UI risk across three places. The format-helper consolidation already delivered the bigger consolidation win (~150 LOC across 9 files vs the projected ~80 LOC for the cards). (c) Step 8's "builder functions for inline findings" cleanup deferred — the union shape change is the high-value bit; per-finding builders are scope creep that doesn't affect behavior.
- **Apply result preview**: Bundled-skill applies now render a file tree instead of a flat `<pre>` text block. `ApplyResult.diffPreview` preserved for backward compatibility.
- **DB schema v12**: three new tables — `mcp_scan_runs`, `mcp_scan_findings` (FK cascades on run delete, indexes on `server_id` and `run_id`), `mcp_tool_fingerprints` (composite PK `server_id + tool_name` avoids NULL footgun).
- **Wave 10.2a — Cluster X (part 1): Multi-platform adapter architecture.** TODO #223.
  - New `SessionAdapter` interface + registry (`src/lib/adapters/`) with `discover()`, `parseFile()`, `parseFileWithMeta?()`. `claude` adapter wraps existing parser/ingest paths — no behavior change, only formalization.
  - `enabledAdapters?: string[]` on `MinderConfig` (default `["claude"]`). `PATCH /api/config` validates adapter IDs against the registry; rejects unknown IDs with 400.
  - `source` field threaded through `UsageTurn`, `SessionSummary`, `SessionDetail`, `SessionRow`. All existing sessions coerce to `"claude"`.
  - **By Source** breakdown on `/usage` — always visible when data exists (proves the pipeline end-to-end with one "Claude Code" row today). `bySource: SourceBreakdown[]` on `UsageReport`, computed by both file-parse and DB aggregation paths.
  - **Source badge** (`SourceBadge`) in session row and session header — always visible; shows "Claude Code" for all current sessions.
  - **Source filter** dropdown in Sessions browser toolbar — always visible when sessions exist.
  - **Adapters** section in Settings — lists all registered adapters with enable/disable toggle and status badge.
  - `?source=` query param on `/api/sessions` and `/api/usage` (cache key + ETag). `/api/sessions` also gates results by `enabledAdapters` config — disabling an adapter produces an empty list.
  - Help doc at `/settings#adapters`.
- **DB schema v11**: `sessions.source TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'claude'` + `idx_sessions_source` index. Existing rows migrated to `'claude'` automatically — no re-parse required.
- Settings → Notifications, Integrations, Terminal, and Auto-title sections now ship with real controls; Wave-1 placeholder cards removed for these four sections.
- `NotificationListener` no longer requests browser notification permission silently on mount. Permission is now requested explicitly via the "Enable browser notifications" button in Settings → Notifications.
- `MinderConfig.telegram` no longer stores `botToken`. Bot tokens now live in `~/.minder/secrets.json` (key: `telegram.bot_token`). Only `chatId` remains in the public config.
- **`walkSkills.ts`** now traverses `~/.claude/skills-disabled/` in addition to `~/.claude/skills/` and tags entries with `disabled: true`. Disabled entries appear in the catalog and skill API responses, enabling the toggle UI to reflect current state without a separate lookup.
- AppNav **Hooks** entry now links to `/hooks` (top-level browser) instead of `/config?type=hooks`. The `/config` Hooks tab is unchanged.

### Fixed
- **`writeFileAtomic` now retries Windows EPERM/EBUSY renames (issue #105).** `writeFileAtomic` in `src/lib/atomicWrite.ts` finished its tmp+rename dance with a raw `fs.rename`, which intermittently failed on Windows with `EPERM: operation not permitted, rename` when parallel work churned the filesystem (handle-release lag) — surfacing as a flaky `applyPlugin` test and, in production, a rare lost config/TODO.md/settings.json write. It now routes through the sibling `renameWithRetry` (linear backoff over `EBUSY`/`EPERM`/`ENOTEMPTY`, already used by the DB quarantine path), making this the codebase's single rename helper for the hot write path. No-op on the fast, uncontended path. New `tests/atomicWrite.test.ts` covers happy-path round-trips, Buffer byte-fidelity, a transient-EPERM retry that succeeds on the second attempt, immediate throw on non-transient `ENOENT` (with tmp cleanup), and `renameWithRetry` giving up after N attempts.
- **Live-session liveness: CLI ground-truth now flows into Agent View / Kanban (issues #152, #153, #156, #157).** Four follow-ups from the T1.1 `claude agents --json` integration. (#152) `src/lib/agentView/aggregate.ts` hardcoded `runningProcess: false` in its hook-only and pure-JSONL branches, so a genuinely-running foreground session that the CLI confirmed alive (`isLive === true`) still rendered as "not running" on the Agent View / Kanban / live-cost cards — contradicting the ProjectCard "live" badge for the same session. Both branches now derive `runningProcess`/`livenessSource` from the CLI signal via a new pure helper `resolveCliLiveness(isLive, fallbackSource)`: `isLive === true` ⇒ `runningProcess: true` + new `livenessSource: "cli"`; `false`/`undefined` preserve the prior `false` + fallback source (so older Claude Code installs with no `isLive` are unchanged). The confirmed `pid` is also threaded onto `LiveAgentSession`. (#153) `src/lib/claudeAgentsCli.ts` stamped `cachedAt` *after* the CLI call resolved, so a slow fetch silently widened the effective staleness window past the documented 10 s (TTL + fetch latency); the timestamp is now sampled *before* the fetch starts, measuring staleness from the data's actual sample point. (#156) `src/components/StatusDashboard.tsx` carried a local `StatusPayload` interface that drifted from the canonical one in `liveStatus.ts` (missing `cliAvailable`), silently dropping the field at the `as` cast; it now imports the canonical type. (#157) `getLiveStatusPayload`'s readdir-error path cached an empty payload for the full 6 s API window when the CLI was available; `buildStatusPayload` now tags error payloads `transient` and the cache write is skipped for them, so the next ≤5 s poll rebuilds instead of pinning the empty state. Tests: new `resolveCliLiveness` coverage of all three `isLive` states in `tests/agentView_aggregate.test.ts`; new fake-timer test in `tests/claudeAgentsCli.test.ts` proving a 4 s fetch + 7 s wait (11 s > 10 s TTL) re-fetches despite the cache being written only 7 s ago.
- **MCP test suite isolation: ~/.claude/projects/ + scan-cache priming + DB path (issue #173 Problem A).** Three MCP test files (`mcpServer`, `mcpResources`, `mcpTools`) previously ran without any filesystem isolation — they walked the developer's real `~/.claude/projects/` directory (281 sessions / 761 MiB on the maintainer's machine), the configured devRoot (`C:\dev` with ~61 real projects on Windows), AND opened the real `~/.minder/index.db` because `DB_DIR`/`DB_PATH` in `src/lib/db/connection.ts` are computed at module load time. Result: `list-projects` took 60.9s, `minder://stats` took 63.2s, and the entire MCP suite ran 77s consistently — flaky under vitest worker contention and prone to blowing the SDK request timeout (#158). Fix lives entirely in tests: new shared helper `tests/_helpers/mcpIsolation.ts` exposes `installMcpIsolation("perTest" | "perFile")` which (1) overrides `process.env.HOME`/`USERPROFILE` to a fresh tmp dir with an empty `.claude/projects/` and spies `os.homedir`, (2) drops globalThis singletons (`__minderDb`, `__scanCache`, `__usageCache`, `__usageFileCache`, `__usageAllSessionsInFlight`, `__minderMcpScanInFlight`, `__sessionsCache`, `__sessionIndex`), (3) calls `vi.resetModules()` so any subsequent dynamic import of `@/lib/db/connection` re-captures `DB_PATH` with the spied homedir, (4) pre-populates the scan cache with an empty `ScanResult` so `getCachedOrFreshScan` short-circuits the devRoot walk, and (5) runs `initDb()` against the fresh tmp DB so OTEL/usage queries return empty results instead of `no such table` errors. Each MCP test file's `client()` helper now uses `await import("@/lib/mcp/server")` instead of a static import so the dynamic load happens AFTER `vi.resetModules()`. Empirical post-fix timings (in isolation, `--pool=forks`): `list-projects` **165ms** (369× faster), `minder://stats` **237ms** (267× faster), `minder://usage/7d` **122ms** (28× faster), `get-usage-by-day` **118ms** (45× faster), `OTEL tools` 59-73ms each, MCP suite total **8.07s** (9.6× faster). Full test suite duration **54.6s** vs. the issue-reported 100-488s range. **No production code touched.** Note: issue #173 also claimed a second problem family (data-façade "file backend" tests timing out from real-dir walks); empirical probing proved that diagnosis wrong — those tests correctly isolate, the 8-9s wall time is module-import overhead from `vi.resetModules()` re-importing the facade per test. Tracked separately as #175.
- **Session detail + list DB loaders: parity gap on `isWorktree`, `source`, `workMode` (issue #172).** `loadSessionDetailFromDb` in `src/lib/data/sessionDetailFromDb.ts` silently returned `undefined` for three `SessionSummary` fields that the file-parse path populates correctly: `isWorktree`, `source`, and `workMode`. The fields are optional on `SessionDetail extends SessionSummary` so TS never flagged the omission, but in DB mode the worktree badge, adapter-attribution chip (Wave 10.2a), and work-mode bar all silently disappeared from session detail pages. Detail loader now SELECTs `source` + the four `work_mode_*_pct` columns and composes the same shape the list loader produces. While verifying parity, discovered the list loader was ALSO broken for `isWorktree`: `src/lib/db/ingest.ts:920` stores the canonicalized `project_dir_name` (with `--claude-worktrees-*` stripped by `canonicalizeDirName` to group worktree sessions under the parent project's slug), so both loaders' previous `isWorktreeEncodedDir(project_dir_name)` calls always returned `false`. Fix: new helper `isWorktreeFilePath` in `src/lib/scanner/worktreeCheck.ts` derives the worktree fact from the raw `file_path` column (which threads through unchanged from `walkProjects` and preserves the worktree marker). Both DB loaders updated to use it. Empirical verification: on the maintainer's index, 0 sessions previously carried `--claude-worktrees-` in `project_dir_name`; the new derivation correctly classifies new worktree sessions via their raw filesystem path. 2 new tests: `dataSessionDetail.test.ts` asserts the three-field parity with stamped non-default values (`source='codex'`, custom workmode percentages, worktree dir name); `dataSessionsList.test.ts` adds a dedicated worktree-detection regression test driving a session inside a `--claude-worktrees-*` dir through both backends and asserting `isWorktree === true` on each.
- **PR #167 review feedback — 4 carryover Copilot comments.** (1) `src/lib/db/schema.sql` header comment bumped from "version 12" to "version 14" to match the actual migration count (last migration at `migrations.ts:406`). (2) `loadSessionDetailFromDb` in `src/lib/data/sessionDetailFromDb.ts` now populates `SessionDetail.prs` from a small indexed SELECT against `session_prs` ordered by `pr_number ASC`, matching the list-loader pattern in `sessionsListFromDb.ts:267-269`. Pre-fix the DB path silently returned `prs: undefined` for every session — losing the PR chips on session detail pages when `MINDER_USE_DB=1` even though the file-parse path populated them correctly. (3) `docs/help/sessions.md` and (4) `public/help/sessions.md` line 58 wording corrected from "Chips appear in encounter order" to "Chips are ordered by PR number ascending" — the actual implementation has always sorted by PR number (file-parse via `Array.prototype.sort` on numeric `number` field; DB path via SQL `ORDER BY pr_number`), the docs were wrong.
- **`/agents` per-agent cost column — replaced dead JSONL walk with OTEL rollup (issue #161).** Pre-PR, `src/lib/usage/agentCost.ts` walked `~/.claude/projects/**/*.jsonl` looking for sidechain assistant entries linked via `parentToolUseID`. Claude Code ~v2.1.150 dropped sidechain entries from the parent session's JSONL (probed 2026-05-25: 0/214 sessions on disk retain any `isSidechain: true` assistant entry), so the walk silently returned `$0` for every agent on the `/agents` page. New module `src/lib/usage/agentCostFromOtel.ts` queries `otel_events` for `subagent_completed` invocations and joins to `api_request` rows filtered by `query_source LIKE 'agent:%'` (the per-call disambiguator we missed in T1.2). For each prompt.id, cost is distributed across the matched set of invocations proportionally by `total_tokens`: `agent:builtin:X` rows go only to invocations whose `agent_type = X`; `agent:custom` rows go to invocations whose `agent_type` is not in any builtin set referenced in that prompt. Single-invocation prompts collapse to share=1.0 (no behavior change for the easy case). `computeAgentCostFromFiles()` retains its public name and Map<agent_name, AgentCostEntry> contract — only the implementation now uses OTEL. Coverage caveat surfaced in `docs/help/agents.md` + `public/help/agents.md`: the chip shows `$0` for pre-OTEL sessions (most of any user's history) and real numbers for sessions run with `OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT` configured. Empirical verification: `/api/agents` went from `0/67 with cost > $0` (pre-fix) to `14/67 with cost > $0` ($112.83 attributed sum).
- **Subagents tab overcounting in parallel-dispatch turns (T1.2 followup).** The original T1.2 ship (PR #162) attributed cost by looking up `api_request` rows by `subagent_completed.prompt.id` and assigning the full result to each invocation. Discovered during #161 investigation that Claude Code's `prompt.id` is a per-user-turn identifier, not per-subagent: a single user prompt that dispatches N agents in parallel produces N `subagent_completed` rows that all share one `prompt.id`, AND every `api_request` from any of those agents (plus the main thread) carries that same `prompt.id`. Net effect on `/sessions/<id>`: an 18-way parallel dispatch turn showed all 18 agent rows with identical `$77.98 · 787.9k tok` chips. Replacement: `enrichSubagentsFromOtel` now delegates to the new `agentCostFromOtel` util, which applies the matched-set proportional-distribution rule described above. Each invocation's per-row chip now reflects its own token share. Verified visually: the same 18-row turn now shows 17 distinct cost values ranging from $0.95 to $9.04. 4 new test cases in `tests/subagentMetrics.test.ts` (proportional split, repl_main_thread exclusion, builtin/custom co-mingle, no-api-request fallback); the old `tests/agentCost.test.ts` JSONL-mock fixture rewritten to OTEL fixtures (9 new tests).
- **PR #162 review feedback — 6 corrections from Codex + Copilot.** Resolves all inline review comments in one follow-up commit: (1) Both OTEL queries in `subagentEnrichment.ts` now filter on the indexed `otel_events.session_id` column instead of `json_extract(payload_json, '$.attrs."session.id"')`. Catches the Codex P1 (missing per-record attrs when ingest sourced `session_id` from resource attrs) AND removes the full-table-scan that defeated the `otel_events_by_session(session_id, ts)` index — matches the convention already used in `src/lib/db/otelQueries.ts`. Test fixture updated to populate the column on INSERT. (2) `SessionSubagents` now imports `formatCostCompact` from `@/lib/format` instead of the local helper that emitted `$0.50¢`-style double-unit strings for sub-cent amounts. (3) `SubagentInfo` doc comment updated to describe the OTEL data path (was stale — still claimed sidechain-JSONL + file-parse-only). (4) Added dedicated `totalTokens` field instead of overloading `inputTokens` with the api_request-less rollup total — prevents silent double-counting if a future consumer reads both. UI renders the token chip from `inputTokens + outputTokens` when present, falls back to `totalTokens` otherwise. (5) Duration-chip tooltip reworded — no longer claims "sidechain turn" provenance for OTEL-derived metrics. (6) Same indexed-column fix on the api_request rollup query.
- **PR #159 review feedback — 8 corrections from Copilot + Codex automated review.** Resolves all inline review comments without leaving follow-up issues open: (1) `isLiveProcess` typeguard now validates `(name === undefined || typeof name === "string")` so non-string names can't leak into `processName: string` (closes #150). (2) `invalidateClaudeAgentsCache()` clears `__claudeAgentsFlight` and the in-flight `.then()` skips the cache write when its flight identity no longer matches — eliminating the post-invalidation stale-repopulation race (closes #149). (3) `liveStatus.ts` sort now applies an `isLive` tiebreaker (live → undefined → dead) inside each status bucket, so a CLI-confirmed-live working session sorts above a dead-but-recent approval session for the same slug (closes #151). (4) `getLiveStatusPayload()` uses a 1 s `API_CACHE_TTL_CLI_UNAVAILABLE` when the cached payload has `cliAvailable === false`, matching the inner CLI null-result TTL so transient CLI blips recover within 1 s instead of being pinned for the full 6 s API window. (5) `ProjectCard.LiveStatusBadge` gains a `cliAvailable` prop; the awaiting branch now requires `(isVerifiedLive || !cliAvailable)` so a crashed-while-awaiting session falls through to the dim "live?" badge instead of showing amber "input" with no live process behind it (closes #148). (6) Both `LiveStatusBadge` call sites pass `cliAvailable={snapshot.cliAvailable}`. (7) `PulseProvider` gates the `verifiedLiveSlugs ?? liveSlugs` fallback on `cliAvailable` (closes #154). (8) `PulseProvider` sorts `liveSlugs`/`awaitingSlugs`/`verifiedLiveSlugs` on receipt so the index-pairwise equality check doesn't trigger a re-render on Set-derived order-only churn (closes #155). 2 new tests in `tests/claudeAgentsCli.test.ts` cover the non-string-name rejection and the invalidate-during-flight race.
- **Build — pin `zod` to v3.25.76 for MCP SDK type compatibility.** The pnpm migration (introduced via `pnpm.onlyBuiltDependencies` + `pnpm-workspace.yaml`) resolved transitive `zod@4.4.3` for our top-level imports while `@modelcontextprotocol/sdk@1.29.0` declared a peer of `zod@^3.25 || ^4.0`. The two versions' types didn't unify across the SDK's `ZodRawShapeCompat` boundary, leading to `TS2322 'ZodOptional<ZodString>' is not assignable to AnySchema` cascades across every `registerTool({ inputSchema: { ... } })` call site (12 files in `src/lib/mcp/tools/*` and `src/mcp/screenshot-to-code/`). Pinning `zod: 3.25.76` as a direct dependency plus `pnpm.overrides.zod` + npm `overrides.zod` forces the SDK and our code onto the same Zod version. New `pnpm-lock.yaml` committed.
- **T1.1 follow-up — top-5 code review findings.** Five correctness fixes layered on top of the `claude agents --json` integration: (1) `liveStatus.ts` merge loop now wraps `new Date(proc.startedAt).toISOString()` in `try/catch` AND the `isLiveProcess` typeguard rejects non-finite `startedAt`; a single CLI entry with NaN/Infinity/out-of-range can no longer abort the merge mid-iteration. (2) `liveStatus.ts` now fetches `getLiveProcesses()` concurrently with the FS walk and uses its session-id set to override the `SESSION_MAX_AGE_MS` (4h) skip — long-idle but still-running Claude sessions are kept in `sessions[]` and tagged `isLive=true` instead of being silently dropped. (3) `/api/pulse` `approvalCount` now excludes `s.isLive === false`, so the bell badge no longer inflates from CLI-confirmed-dead approval sessions whose JSONL is still fresh. (4) `claudeAgentsCli.ts` caches `null` results for only 1 s (new `CACHE_TTL_NULL_MS`) instead of the full 10 s `CACHE_TTL_MS`, so a transient CLI failure can't lock the dashboard into fallback mode for an entire TTL window.
